English: The emperor issued an imperial edict ordering Guo Ziyi to lead 30,000 troops to defend the town of Fenyang from the river, and the capital was placed under martial law.

古文：戊午夜，白雾起西北竟天。
现代文：十一日夜，白雾从西北起来布满天空。
English: On the night of the 11th, a white mist rose from the northwest and covered the sky.

古文：子仪移镇奉天。
现代文：郭子仪从泾阳移军队镇守奉天。
English: Guo Ziyi moved troops from Shenyang to guard Fengtian.

古文：乙丑昼，有大流星出于午，没于亥。
现代文：十八日白昼，有个大流星从中午一点出来，半夜二十三点才隐没。
English: On the 18th day of the month, in broad daylight, a large meteor appeared at one o'clock in the afternoon, and did not disappear until midnight on the 23rd.

古文：命左丞李涵宣慰河北。
现代文：命令左丞李涵安抚河北。
English: He ordered General of the Left Li Han to pacify Hebei.

古文：荧惑犯南斗。
现代文：荧惑星侵犯南斗星。
English: Fluorescent planet encroaches on the Southern Dipper.

古文：辛未，靺鞨使来朝。
现代文：二十四日，使者前来朝见。
English: On the 24th, the emissary came to see me in the morning.

古文：桂州山獠陷州城，刺史李良遁去。
现代文：桂州山獠攻陷州县，刺史李良逃走。
English: Guizhou Shanshan invaded Zhoushu County, stabbed Shi Li Liang and fled.

古文：十月戊寅，灵州奏破吐蕃二万，京师解严。
现代文：十月一日，灵州上奏章，攻破吐蕃人马两万，京师解除戒严。
English: On October 1st, Lingshou issued a proclamation, breaking through the 20,000-strong crowd, and Beijing lifted the martial law.

古文：甲申，减京官职田三分之一，给军粮。
现代文：七日，减少在京官员禄米田三分之一，用来供给军粮。
English: On the 7th, a third of the rice fields allocated to officials in Beijing were reduced to supply military rations.

古文：乙酉，醴泉出于栎阳，饮之愈疾。
现代文：八日，有甘泉从栎阳流出，饮了以后可以治病。
English: On the eighth day, there was a sweet spring flowing out of Shenyang. After drinking it, you can cure yourself.

古文：其侍中、中书令宜升入正二品，门下、中书侍郎升入正三品。 
现代文：回纥、党项派遣使者前来朝见。二十六日，皇上驾到紫宸殿，当面出策论考试茂才异行、安贫乐道、孝悌力田、高蹈不仕等四科举人。十一月十四日，依旧改黄门侍郎为门下侍郎。
English: On the 26th, the Emperor drove to Shishinden, and in front of the Emperor, he held a four-subject examination, including Shosei-hitsugyo, Anpo-le-do, Takahata-ritsa, and Takahata-nushi. On the 14th of November, the Yellow Gate attendant was still changed to the door attendant.

古文：壬戌夜，月晕南北河、东井，镇星入舆鬼，久之方散。
现代文：十六日夜，在天上南北天河、东井星座发生月晕，镇星进入舆鬼星座，很久才散去。
English: On the night of the 16th, a lunar eclipse occurred in the constellations of the South and North Celestial Rivers and the East Well in the sky, and the town star entered the ghost constellation, and it took a long time to disperse.

古文：甲子，月去轩辕一尺。
现代文：十八日，月亮距离轩辕星只一尺。
English: On the 18th, the moon was only one foot away from the star.

古文：己丑，率百官京城士庶出钱以助军。
现代文：十九日，皇上率领百官及京城百姓出钱来助军打仗。
English: On the 19th, the emperor led hundreds of officials and the people of the capital to pay money to help the army fight.

古文：壬申，京师地震，自东北来，其声如雷。
现代文：二十六日，京师地震，开始从东北方向起来，地震声音像打雷。
English: On the 26th, the Beijing earthquake began to rise from the northeast, and the earthquake sounded like thunder.

古文：十二月甲申，凤翔李抱玉来朝。
现代文：十二月八日，凤翔李抱玉前来朝见。
English: On December 8, Fengxiang Li hugged Yu and came to see him in the morning.

古文：丁酉，太原节度使辛云京来朝。
现代文：二十一日，太原节度使辛云京前来朝见。
English: On the twenty-first day of the month, the Taiyuan Festival made Xin Yunjing come to see the morning.

古文：荧惑入壁垒。
现代文：荧惑星进入壁垒星座。
English: The fluorescent planet enters the barrier constellation.

古文：戊戌黑气如尘，竟北方。
现代文：二十二日，黑色气体像尘土，覆盖了整个北方。
English: On the 22nd, the black gas, like dust, covered the entire north.

古文：是秋，河东、河南、淮南、浙江东西、福建等道五十五州奏水灾。
现代文：这年秋天，河东、河南、淮南、浙江东、西、福建等道五十五州水灾。
English: In the autumn of that year, flooding occurred in 55 prefectures, including Hedong, Henan, Huainan, East and West Zhejiang, and Fujian.

古文：三年春正月丙午朔。
现代文：大历三年春正月一日是朔日。
English: The first day of the first month of spring in the third year of the lunar calendar is New Year's Day.

古文：辛亥，剑南西山置乾州，管招武、宁远二县。
现代文：六日，剑南、西山设置乾州，管辖招武、宁远二县。
English: On the 6th, Jiangnan and Xishan were set up as Qianzhou, with jurisdiction over Zhaowu and Ningyuan counties.

古文：壬子夜，月掩毕。
现代文：七日夜晚，月亮遮掩了毕星。
English: On the evening of the seventh day, the moon covered the stars.

古文：甲子，册新罗国王金乾运母为太妃。
现代文：十九日，册封新罗国王金乾运之母为太妃。
English: On the 19th, the mother of King of Silla, King Jin Kianyun, was crowned as Empress Dowager.

古文：甲戌，以工部侍郎蒋涣为尚书左丞，浙西团练观察使、苏州刺史韦元甫为尚书右丞。左丞李涵、右丞贾至并为兵部侍郎。
现代文：二十四日，以工部侍郎蒋涣为尚书左丞，浙西团练观察使、苏州刺史韦元甫为尚书右丞，左丞李涵、右丞贾至都为兵部侍郎。
English: On the twenty-fourth day, the attendant of the Ministry of Industry, Jiang Jie, was appointed as the attendant of the Ministry of War as the attendant of the Ministry of War, the observer of the Western Zhejiang Reunification and the observer of the Western Suzhou Reunification as the attendant of the Ministry of War, the attendant of the Ministry of War as the attendant of the Ministry of War as the attendant of the Ministry of War, and the attendant of the Ministry of War as the attendant of the Ministry of War.

古文：乙亥，永和公主薨。
现代文：三十日，永和公主去世。
English: On the 30th, Princess Yonghe passed away.

古文：二月己卯，以常州刺史李栖筠为苏州刺史、兼御史中丞、浙西团练观察使。
现代文：二月四日，以常州刺史李栖筠为苏州刺史、兼御史中丞、浙江团练观察使。
English: On February 4th, Li Qianqian, the historian of Changzhou, was appointed as the historian of Suzhou, as well as the vice-president of history, and the observer of the group exercise in Zhejiang.

古文：壬午，邠宁节度使马璘来朝。
现代文：七日，宁节度使马瞞前来朝见。
English: On the seventh day, Ning Jiedu asked Ma Xie to come and see him in the morning.

古文：三月乙巳朔，日有蚀之。
现代文：三月一日，有日蚀。
English: On March 1st, there will be a solar eclipse.

古文：壬申，割恆州行唐县置泜州，以灵寿、恆阳隶之。
现代文：二十八日，分割开恒州行唐县而设氵氐州，使灵寿、恒阳隶属它管辖。
English: On the 28th, Hengzhou and Tang County were split off to form Ganzhou, and Lingshou and Hengyang were placed under its jurisdiction.

古文：夏四月戊寅，以山南西道节度使、邓国公张献诚为检校户部尚书。以疾辞位也。
现代文：夏四月四日，以山南西道节度使、邓国公张献诚为检校户部尚书，因为他以疾病辞去节度使职位。
English: On the 4th day of the 4th month of the summer, Deng Guokong Zhang Xiancheng, the festival secretary of Shannan West Road, was appointed as the inspector of the school, because he resigned from the post of festival secretary due to illness.

古文：右羽林将军张献恭为梁州刺史、兼御史中丞，充山南西道节度观察使。兄献诚所荐也。
现代文：右羽林将军张献恭为梁州刺史、兼任御史中丞，充任山南西道节度观察使，这是由他的哥哥张献诚所推荐。
English: Zhang Xianqiong, the general of the Right Uhlin, was appointed as the chief historian of Liangzhou, concurrently served as the vice-president of the imperial history, and served as the observer of the Shannan West Road festival, which was recommended by his brother Zhang Xiancheng.

古文：壬寅，滑亳节度使令狐彰加检校工部尚书。
现代文：二十八日，滑、亳节度使令狐彰给予检校工部尚书的加官。
English: On the 28th day of the month, with the arrival of the Spring Festival and the Mid-Autumn Festival, Ling Foo-Chang was given the additional post of inspector of the inspection department.

古文：剑南西川节度使、兼御史大夫崔旰来朝。
现代文：剑南、西川节度使、兼御史大夫崔旰前来朝见。
English: Jian'nan, Nishikawa Setsudo's envoy, and Goshi no daifu Cui Yao came to see him in the morning.

古文：五月戊申，加崔旰检校右散骑常待。
现代文：五月五日，赐给崔旰检校右散骑常侍的加官。
English: On May 5th, Choe Son Gyeong Gwan was given the additional post of Right Hand Cavalryman.

古文：乙卯，追谥故齐王倓为承天皇帝，兴信公主亡女张氏为恭顺皇后，祔葬。
现代文：十二日，追加谥号给齐王亻炎为 承天皇帝 ，追谥兴信公主已死去的女儿张氏为 恭顺皇后 ，两人一起合葬。
English: On the 12th, the additional honorary title was given to Qi Wang Benyan as the Emperor Chengtian, and the deceased daughter of Princess Xingxin Zhang as the Empress Gongshun, and the two were buried together.

古文：辛酉，改桂州临源县为全义县。
现代文：十八日，改桂州临源县为全义县。
English: On the 18th, Guizhou Linyuan County was changed to QuanYi County.

古文：癸酉，以左散骑常侍崔昭为京兆尹。
现代文：三十日，以左散骑常侍崔昭为京兆尹。
English: On the 30th, the left horseback riding attendant Cui Zhao became Jing Zhaoyun.

古文：是日地震。
现代文：这天地震。
English: There was an earthquake that day.

古文：戊辰，以剑南西川节度使崔旰检校工部尚书，改名宁。宁为柏茂林、杨子琳所攻，宁既入朝，子琳乘虚袭据成都府。
现代文：二十五日，以剑南西川节度使崔旰为检校工部尚书，改名为宁，崔宁被柏林茂、杨子琳所攻打，崔宁已经入朝做官，杨子琳乘虚袭击并占领了成都府。
English: On the 25th, the Jian'nan Xichuan Festival was used to make Cui Yao the inspector of the inspection department of Shangshu, and changed his name to Ning. Cui Ning was attacked by Berlin Mao and Yang Zilin. Cui Ning had already entered the court as an official, and Yang Zilin took advantage of the false attack and occupied Chengdu Prefecture.

古文：朝廷忧之，即日诏宁还成都。
现代文：朝廷为此十分忧虑，当日便下诏命令崔宁返回成都。
English: The imperial court was very worried about this, and on the same day issued an edict ordering Cui Ning to return to Chengdu.

古文：庚午，以邛州剌史鲜于叔明为梓州刺史，充剑南东川节度使。
现代文：二十七日，以邛州刺史鲜于叔明为梓州刺史，充任剑南东川节度使。
English: On the 27th, Shen Yu Shuming, the chief historian of Zhangzhou, was appointed as the chief historian of Zizhou, and served as the chief envoy to the Jian'nan Dongchuan Festival.

古文：六月戊子，承天皇帝祔奉天皇帝庙，同殿异室，庚寅，太子少师王玙卒。
现代文：六月六日，承天皇帝的灵位附在奉天皇帝庙中合祭，两个神位同殿而不同室。八日，太子少师王王与去世。
English: On June 6, the spiritual throne of Emperor Jingtian was attached to the Fengtian Emperor Temple for the festival, and the two divine thrones were in the same hall but in different rooms. On the 8th, the young prince Wang Wang passed away.

古文：壬辰，幽州节度使、检校侍中、幽州大都督府长史李怀仙为麾下兵马使硃希彩所杀。
现代文：十日，幽州节度使、检校侍中、幽州大都督府长史李怀仙被部下兵马使朱希彩所杀。
English: On the 10th day of the month, Shi Lihuaixian, Yuzhou's festival envoy, inspector of schools, and Yuzhou's governor, was killed by Zhu Xisai, a subordinate envoy.

古文：庚子，淮南节度使检校尚书左仆射、知省事、扬州大都督府长史、赵国公崔圆卒。
现代文：二十八日，淮南节度使、检校尚书左仆射、主持尚书省事、扬州大都督府长史、赵国公崔圆去世。
English: On the 28th, Zhao Guogong Cui Yuan, Minister of Huainan Festival, Inspector of Schools Shang Shuxi Zuo Fu Sha, Moderator of Shang Shuxi Provincial Affairs, Governor of Yangzhou, passed away.

古文：闰月己酉，郭子仪加司徒。
现代文：闰六月七日，又给予郭子仪司徒的加官。
English: On the 7th day of the 6th month, Guo Zi Yi was also given the additional post of the leader.

古文：庚申，宰臣充河南副元帅王缙兼幽州节度使。
现代文：十八日，宰辅之臣充任河南副元帅王缙兼任幽州节度使。
English: On the 18th, the vassal of the Vice-Marshal of Henan, Wang Qi, was appointed as the Vice-Marshal of Henan and also as the Yuzhou Festival envoy.

古文：以尚书右丞韦元甫扬州大都督府长史，兼御史大夫，充淮南节度观察等使。
现代文：以尚书右丞韦元甫任扬州大都督府长史、兼御史大夫，充任淮南节度使、观察使。
English: Wei Yuanfu, with the title of Shang Shuyuan, served as the governor of Yangzhou and the chief historian, as well as the chief historian, and served as the Huainan Festival envoy and the observation envoy.

古文：西卯，以幽州节度副使、试太常卿硃希彩知幽州留后。
现代文：二十五日，以幽州节度副使、试用太常卿朱希彩主持幽州留后的工作。
English: On the 25th, Zhu Xicai, Vice-Envoy of the Yuzhou Festival and Probationary Grand Marshal, presided over the work after his stay in Yuzhou.

古文：遣兵部侍郎李涵兼御史大夫，使河北宣慰，以幽州乱故也。
现代文：派遣兵部侍郎李涵兼任御史大夫，前往河北安抚，这是因为幽州大乱的原因。
English: He dispatched Li Han, the attendant of the military department, who also served as the chief historian, to pacify Hebei, which was the reason for the Yuzhou Rebellion.

古文：庚午，相州薛嵩、魏州田承嗣、恆州李宝臣并加左右仆射。
现代文：二十八日，相州薛嵩、魏州田承嗣、恒州李宝臣都赐予左仆射或右仆射的加官。
English: On the 28th, Xue Song of Xiangzhou, Tian Heizi of Weizhou, and Li Baochen of Hengzhou were all given additional posts for shooting left-handed or right-handed.

古文：七月壬申，崔宁弟宽攻破杨子琳，收复成都府。
现代文：七月一日，崔宁之弟崔宽攻破杨子琳，收复成都府。
English: On July 1, Cui Nings younger brother Cui Guang defeated Yang Zilin and recovered Chengdu.

古文：是月，五星并聚于东井，占曰：中国之利也。
现代文：这月，金、木、水、火、土五大行星都聚集在东井星座。卜卦的人占卦说： 这是唐王朝有利了。 
English: This month, the five planets of gold, wood, water, fire and earth are gathered in the constellation of the East Well. The fortune-teller said: This is advantageous to the Tang Dynasty.

古文：乙亥，王缙赴镇州。
现代文：四日，王缙奔赴镇州。
English: On the fourth day, Wang Qian rushed to Zhenzhou.

古文：八月己未，月掩毕。
现代文：八月十八日，月亮遮掩毕星。
English: On August 18th, the moon eclipsed the stars.

古文：辛酉，月入东井。
现代文：二十日，月亮进入东井星座。
English: On the 20th, the moon entered the constellation of the East Well.

古文：壬戌，吐蕃十万寇灵武。
现代文：二十一日，吐蕃十万兵入侵灵武。
English: On the 21st, 100,000 soldiers from Tubo invaded Lingwu.

古文：荧或犯太微垣。
现代文：荧惑星侵犯太微垣星座。
English: Fluorescent planet encroaches on the constellation of the Too Small Wall.

古文：丁卯，吐蕃寇邠宁，节度使马璘破吐蕃二万于邠州。
现代文：二十六日，吐蕃入侵州，京师戒严。二十七日，宁节度使马瞞在州攻破吐蕃军队三万之众。
English: On the 26th, the Tubo invaded the prefecture, and the Beijing division was placed under martial law. On the 27th, the Ning Festival made Ma Xizhe break through the 30,000 troops of the Tubo army in the prefecture.

古文：御史大夫崔涣为税地青青钱使。给百官俸钱不平，诏尚书左丞蒋涣按鞫，贬崔涣为道州刺史。
现代文：御史大夫崔涣为税地青苗钱使，由于供给百官薪俸钱不公平，皇上诏令尚书左丞蒋涣检举审讯，贬崔涣为道州刺史。
English: Since the provision of salary money to hundreds of officials was unfair, the emperor issued an imperial edict ordering Shang Shuzhong, the left-hand man of Chiang Kai-shek, to investigate and interrogate, and demoted Cui Wei to the position of prefectural historian.

古文：庚午，河东节度使、检校左仆射、太原尹、同中书门下平章事辛云京卒。
现代文：二十九日，河东节度使、检校左仆射、太原尹、同中书门下平章事辛云京去世。
English: On the 29th day of the month, Xin Yunjing, the festival envoy of Hedong, the school inspector Zuofusa, Taiyuan Yin, and the junior high school student Xia Ping Zhang, passed away.

古文：门下侍郎、同中书门下平章事、兼幽州长史、持节、河南副元帅、都统河南淮西山南东道诸节度行营、兼幽州卢龙等军节度使、太微宫使、弘文馆大学士、兼东都留守、齐国公王缙兼太原尹、北都留守，充河东军节度，余官使并如故。
现代文：门下侍郎、同中书门下平章事、兼幽州长史、持节、河南副元帅、都统河南、淮西、山南东道诸节度行营、兼幽州卢龙等军节度使、太微宫使、弘文馆大学士、兼东都留守、齐国公王缙兼太原尹、北都留守，充任河东军节度使，其余官职使节都像原来一样。
English: His subordinate attendants, subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate subordinate

古文：辛未，以门下侍郎、同中书门下平章事、山剑副元帅、太清宫使、崇玄馆大学士杜鸿渐兼东都留守。
现代文：三十日，以门下侍郎、同中书门下平章事、山、剑副元帅、太清宫使、崇玄馆大学士杜鸿渐兼任东都留守。
English: On the 30th, Du Hongxian, who concurrently held the posts of junior chamberlain, junior secretary of the same school, deputy marshal of the mountain, deputy marshal of the sword, palace envoy of the Taiqing Dynasty, and scholar of the Chongyuan Museum, was absent from Dongdu.

古文：九月壬申。郭子仪自河中移镇奉天。
现代文：九月一日，郭子仪率军从河中移兵镇守奉天。
English: On September 1, Guo Ziyi and his army moved from the middle of the river to guard the town of Fengtian.

古文：岁星入舆鬼。
现代文：岁星进入舆鬼星座。
English: The year star enters the constellation of the ghost.

古文：丁丑，济王环薨。
现代文：六日，济王环去世。
English: On the 6th, Ji Wanghuan passed away.

古文：荧惑入太微垣。
现代文：荧惑星进入太微垣星座。
English: The fluorescent planet enters the constellation of the Great Wall.

古文：壬午，吐蕃寇灵州。
现代文：十一日，吐蕃入侵灵州。
English: On the 11th, the Tuoba invaded Lingzhou.

古文：甲申，以尚书左丞蒋涣为华州刺史，充镇国军潼关防御使。
现代文：十三日，以尚书左丞蒋涣为华州刺史，充任镇国军潼关防御使。
English: On the 13th, with Shang Shuzhanzhong Jiang Qi as the historian of Huazhou, he served as the defense envoy of the town and country army of Shaoguan.

古文：丙戌，检校户部尚书、知省事、邓国公张献诚卒。
现代文：十五日，检校户部尚书、主持尚书省事、邓国公张献诚去世。
English: On the 15th, the head of the inspection department of the school, Shang Shu, the chairman of the inspection department, and Deng Guokong Zhang Xiancheng passed away.

古文：丁亥。工部尚书赵国珍卒。
现代文：十六日，工部尚书赵国珍去世。
English: On the 16th, Zhao Guozhen passed away.

古文：庚寅，以华州刺史张重光为尚书左丞。
现代文：十九日，以前任华州刺史张重光为尚书左丞。
English: On the 19th, Zhang Jiguang, the former vice-governor of Huazhou, became the vice-governor of Shangshu.

古文：壬辰，灵州将白元光破吐蕃二万于灵武。
现代文：二十一日，灵州将白元光在灵武攻破吐蕃二万多军队。
English: On the twenty-first day, Lingshou defeated Baiyuan Guang in Lingwu and drove out more than twenty thousand troops.

古文：戊戌，灵武奏破吐蕃六万，百僚称贺，京师解严。
现代文：二十七日，灵武唐军上奏说攻破吐蕃军队六万，百官祝贺，京师解除戒严。
English: On the 27th, the Lingwu Tang army reported that it had defeated the 60,000-strong Tubo army. Hundreds of officials congratulated, and the Beijing division lifted the martial law.

古文：冬十月甲寅，朔方留后、灵武大都督府长史常廉光加检校工部尚书。
现代文：冬十月十四日，朔方留后、灵武大都督府长史常谦光赐予检校工部尚书的加官。
English: In the winter of October 14th, after Shuo Fang left, Lingwu Dadu Governor Shi Chang Qianguang gave Shang Shu's promotion to the inspection department of the school.

古文：乙未，以京兆尹李勉为广州刺史，充岭南节度使。
现代文：十九日，以京兆尹李勉为广州刺史，充任岭南节度使。
English: On the 19th, with Jing Zhaoyun and Li Mian as the history of Guangzhou, he was appointed as the Lingnan Festival envoy.

古文：丁卯，子仪自奉天来朝。
现代文：二十七日，郭子仪从奉天前来朝见。
English: On the 27th, Guo Ziyi came from Mingtian to see the emperor.

古文：十一月丁亥，幽州留后硃希彩为幽州长史，充幽州卢龙节度使，癸巳，加廊下百官厨料，增旧五分之一。
现代文：十一月五日，幽州留后朱希彩为幽州长史，并充任幽州、卢龙节度使。二十三日，赐给殿廊下侍候的百官厨房食料，比旧有的增加五分之一。
English: On November 5th, after Zhu Xicai stayed in Yuzhou, he became the governor of Yuzhou, and served as the Yuzhou and Lulong Festival envoy. On the 23rd, he gave the hundred official kitchen food to waiters under the hallway, an increase of one-fifth compared to the old one.

古文：十二月壬寅，道州刺史崔涣卒。
现代文：十二月二日，道州刺史崔涣去世。
English: On December 2nd, the Daozhou assassin Cui Xuan passed away.

古文：己酉，以邠宁节度使马璘为泾原节度，移镇泾州，其邠宁割隶朔方军。
现代文：九日，以宁节度使马瞞为泾原节度使，移兵镇守泾州，宁军分给朔方军管辖。
English: On the 9th, the Ning Festival made Ma Xie the commander of the Xingyuan Festival, moved troops to guard Zhangzhou, and the Ning Army was assigned to the jurisdiction of the Shuo Army.

古文：邠州将吏以烧马坊为乱，兵马使段秀实斩其凶首八人，方定。
现代文：州将官以烧马厩制造混乱，兵马使段秀实斩了为首凶犯八人，州这才安定。
English: The state generals created chaos by burning stables, and the soldiers and horses made Duan Xiusheng behead eight criminals as the leader, and the state was stable.

古文：四年春正月庚午朔。
现代文：大历四年春正月一日是朔日。
English: The first day of the first month of spring in the fourth year of the lunar calendar is New Year's Day.

古文：甲戌，大风。
现代文：五日，大风。
English: On the fifth day, the wind picked up.

古文：乙亥，大雪，平地盈尺。
现代文：六日，下大雪，平地下雪满满一尺高。
English: On the 6th, it snowed heavily, and the snow on the ground was over a foot high.

古文：甲申，日有蚀之。
现代文：十五日，有日蚀。
English: On the 15th, there will be a solar eclipse.

古文：子仪回河中。
现代文：郭子仪回到河中。
English: Guo Ziyi returned to the river.

古文：戊子，敕有司定王公士庶每户税钱，分上、中、下三等。
现代文：十九日，皇上命令有关部门确定王公、士子、庶人百姓每户缴纳的税钱，交税分上、中、下三等。
English: On the 19th, the emperor ordered the relevant departments to determine the amount of tax paid by princes, nobles and commoners in each household, and to pay tax in the upper, middle and lower tiers.

古文：宗室颍州刺史李岵专杀，法司以议亲，宜赐自尽。
现代文：宗室颍川刺史李岵擅自杀人，审判官员议罪，认为是皇家宗室，应该赐他自尽。
English: Court officials found the family of the royal family guilty of committing suicide. They believed that the family of the royal family should be given the right to commit suicide.

古文：乙未，福建观察使李承昭请徙汀州于长汀县之白石村，从之。黑衣大食国使朝贡。
现代文：二十六日，福建观察使李承昭请求把汀州迁到长汀县之白石村，皇上听从了这个建议，黑衣大食国派使者前来朝贡。
English: On the 26th, the Fujian Observer sent Li Chengzhao to request the transfer of Tingzhou to Baishi Village in Changting County. The emperor listened to this suggestion and sent an envoy to pay tribute.

古文：二月乙巳，以泸州刺史杨子琳为陕州刺史。
现代文：二月六日，以泸州刺史杨子琳为陕州刺史。
English: On February 6th, Yang Zilin from Zhangzhou was appointed as the governor of Shaanxi Province.

古文：乙卯，宰臣杜鸿渐让山剑副元帅，从之。
现代文：十六日，宰辅大臣杜鸿渐辞让山、剑副元帅，皇上同意了。
English: On the 16th, Vice-Minister Du Hongxuan resigned to make Shan and Jian vice-marshals, and the emperor agreed.

古文：丙辰夜，地震，有声如雷者三。
现代文：十七日夜晚，发生地震，地震声音如雷一般响了三次。
English: On the evening of the 17th, an earthquake occurred. The earthquake sounded like thunder three times.

古文：辛酉，以湖南都团练观察使、衡州刺史韦之晋为潭州刺史。因是徙湖南军于潭州。
现代文：二十二日，以湖南都团练观察使、衡州刺史韦之晋为潭州刺史，因此迁移湖南军到潭州。
English: On the 22nd, Hunan's regimental training observation envoy, Hengzhou's Zhishui, was promoted to the post of Tanzhou's Zhishui, so the Hunan army was relocated to Tanzhou.

古文：江西团练使魏少游来朝。
现代文：江西团练使魏少游前来朝见。
English: Jiangxi Rehearsal Makes Wei Shaoyou Come to See the Morning Star.

古文：三月壬申，诏：
现代文：三月四日，皇上下诏曰：
English: On March 4, the Emperor issued the following edict:

古文：夫计人而置官，度事而赋任，因时立制，损益在焉。
现代文： 依据人而设置官吏，根据事而赋予职务，根据时代的特点而订立制度，害处和益处都在这里。
English: The harm and benefit of setting officials according to people, assigning positions according to things, and establishing a system according to the characteristics of the times are all here.

古文：吏足以理人，人足以奉吏，则官称其禄，禄当其秩，然后上下相乐，公私不匮。
现代文：官吏完全可以治理人民，人民完全可以供养官吏，那么官吏的职责和俸禄就相称；俸禄和官职相称，这样以后，上下融洽，公、私双方都不会匮乏。
English: Officials are fully capable of governing the people, and the people are fully capable of supporting officials. Then the duties of officials and their salaries will be commensurate, and the salaries will be commensurate with their official positions. In this way, there will be harmony between the upper and lower levels, and there will be no shortage of both public and private sectors.

古文：昔汉光武时及魏太和中，并减吏员，兼省乡邑，致理之道，此其一隅。
现代文：过去汉光武帝的时代和魏国太和中期，都减少了官员，而且减少和兼并了乡镇，如何治理的方法，这是举一反三的例证。
English: In the past, the era of Emperor Han Guangwu and the mid- and late-periods of the Wei Dynasty, officials were reduced, and townships and townships were reduced and annexed. This is an example of how to govern.

古文：今连岁治戎，天下凋瘵，京师近甸，烦苦尤重，比屋流散，念之恻然。
现代文：现在连年打仗，天下凋敝穷困，京师及附近地区，烦恼困苦尤其严重，很多家室，人们流散，想起来，令人伤感。
English: Now we have been at war for years on end, the country is withered and impoverished, and Beijing and the surrounding areas are particularly troubled and impoverished. Many families and people are scattered, which is sad to think about.

古文：人寡吏多，困于供费，欲其苏息，不可得也，设令廉耻守分，以奉科条，犹有录廪之烦，役使之弊；而况贪猾纵欲，而动逾典章，作威以虐下，厚敛以润已者乎！
现代文：人少官多，供给粮食和费用十分困难，想要让人民休养生息，是不可能的。即使让人民懂得廉耻，敬守本分，奉法守纪，还是有提供禄米的烦扰，还是有役使百姓的弊端。更何况是贪赃奸猾放纵欲望，而且动辄越过法令界限，作威作福来暴虐百姓，残酷剥削苛捐杂税来中饱私囊的呢？
English: There are fewer people and more officials, and it is very difficult to supply food and expenses. It is impossible to let the people rest and recuperate. Even if the people know how to be honest, honor their duties, and abide by the law and discipline, there is still the trouble of providing lumens, and there are still the drawbacks of serving the people. What's more, there are those who are greedy, treacherous, and indulge their desires, and often cross the boundaries of laws and regulations, tyrannize the people by acting as a tyrant, and brutally exploit and tax the people to enrich themselves.

古文：古者县置大夫一员，足以为治，奚必贰佐分掌而后治耶？
现代文：古时县设大夫一名，足够用来治理百姓，哪里需要设置一些副职分掌权力而后治呢？
English: In ancient times, the county set up a doctor, which was enough to govern the people. Where is there a need to set up some deputy posts to hold power and govern later?

古文：且京畿户口，减耗大半，职员如旧，何以堪之？
现代文：再说京师及其附近的户口，减少消耗大半，官职众多仍然像以前一样，国家何以负担得了？
English: Moreover, the number of hukou in Beijing and its vicinity has been reduced by more than half, and the number of government posts remains the same as before. How can the country afford this?

古文：岂可以重困之人，供不给之费。
现代文：难道可以让饱受战乱灾祸的人，供给不需要供给的费用。
English: Is it possible that people who have suffered from the scourge of war can be provided with expenses that do not need to be provided?

古文：使人不倦，其在变通，制事之宜，式从省便。
现代文：要使人们不疲于奔命，关键在于变通，制定政事是否适宜，应检验它是否简省方便。
English: In order to make people work tirelessly, the key lies in flexibility. Whether it is appropriate to formulate policies should be tested to see if it is simple and convenient.

古文：其京兆府长安、万年宜各减丞一员、尉两员，余县各减丞、尉一员。
现代文：现在我命令京兆府之长安、万年两县应各减县丞一名、县尉两名，其余县各减县丞、县尉一名。
English: Now, I order the Chang'an of Jingzhao Prefecture and the two counties of Wanli to each reduce one county magistrate and two county lieutenants, and the remaining counties to each reduce one county magistrate and one county lieutenant.

古文：馀委吏部条件处分。
现代文：其余地方命令吏部根据情况处理。 
English: The remaining local orders will be handled by the cadre department according to the situation.

古文：吏部尚书裴遵庆为右仆射，刘晏改吏部尚书。
现代文：吏部尚书裴遵庆为右仆射，刘晏改任为吏部尚书。
English: Pei Zunqing was appointed as the right-hand man of the secretary of the personnel department, and Liu Xi was appointed as the secretary of the personnel department.

古文：庚寅，江西团练使魏少游封赵国公。
现代文：二十二日，江西团练使魏少游封为赵国公。
English: On the 22nd, the Jiangxi regimental drill promoted Wei Shaoyou to Zhao Guogong.

古文：丙申复置仙州。
现代文：二十八日，重新设置仙州。
English: On the 28th, Xianzhou was re-established.

古文：夏四月壬寅，陕州虞邑县复为安邑县，虢州天平县复为湖城县。
现代文：夏四月四日，陕州虞邑县重又恢复为安邑县，虢州天平县重又恢复为湖城县。
English: On the 4th day of the 4th month of summer, Yuyi County of Shaanxi Province was reinstated as Anyi County, and Tianping County of Ganzhou Province was reinstated as Hucheng County.

古文：五月丙戌，京师地震。
现代文：五月十九日，京师地震。
English: On May 19, the Beijing Chang'an earthquake occurred.

古文：辛卯，以仆固怀恩女为崇徽公主，嫁回纥可汗，仍命兵部侍郎李涵往册命。
现代文：二十四日，皇上以仆固怀恩之女为崇徽公主，嫁给回纥可汗，仍旧命令兵部侍郎李涵前往宣布皇上册封命令。
English: On the twenty-fourth day, the emperor named the daughter of the servant Gu Wai En as the princess of Chonghui, married to Hui Khan, and still ordered Li Han, the attendant of the military department, to go to announce the emperor's appointment order.

古文：六月丁酉，以太子詹事臧希让检校工部尚书，充渭北节度；以渭北节度李光进为太子太保。
现代文：六月一日，以太子詹事臧希让任检校工部尚书，充任渭北节度使；以渭北节度使李光进为太子太保。
English: On June 1st, Emperor Taizong's son, Zhan Shijian Xi, gave up his post as inspector of the School Inspection Department to Shang Shu, and served as the envoy of the Northern Wei Dynasty; with the help of the Northern Wei Dynasty, Li Guangjin became the prince's bodyguard.

古文：自今已后，非灼然蠹害，不得辄加非理，所司严加纠察以闻。
现代文：十五日，升辰州为都督府，分辰、巫、溪、锦、业等州而设置团练观察使。秋七月四日，以澧州刺史崔馞为潭州刺史、湖南团练观察使。十八日，因为天下法官滥用刑法，命令有关部门严加纠察而后向上报告。
English: On the 15th, a group training observation envoy was set up for the prefectural governor of Shentian, and the prefectural governors of Fengtian, Wuxi, Xixi, Jin and Ying. On the 4th of July, a group training observation envoy was set up for the prefectural governor of Hunan and the group training observer for the prefectural governor of Hunan. On the 18th, because of the abuse of criminal law by judges around the world, the relevant departments were ordered to strictly picket and then report to the top.

古文：先是，皇姨弟薛华因酒色之急，手刃三人，弃尸于井，事发系狱，赐自尽，故有是诏。
现代文：先前皇姨弟薛华因为酒色的忿恨，亲手杀了三人，丢尸到井中，事情发生以后，被关押在监狱，赐他自杀，所以才有这道诏令。
English: The imperial edict was issued after the previous emperor's uncle and younger brother, Xue Hua, killed three people with his own hands in a fit of drunken rage and threw the bodies into a well. After the incident, he was imprisoned and told to commit suicide.

古文：八月丙申朔。
现代文：八月一日是朔日。
English: The first day of August is New Year's Day.

古文：自夏四月连雨至此月，京城米斗八百文。
现代文：从夏天四月起连续下雨直到这个月，京城大米每斗八百文。
English: From the summer of April, it rained continuously until this month, and the capital city rice rose by 800 mon per dou.

古文：官出米二万石，减估而粜，以惠贫民。
现代文：官府拿出大米二万石，减价而卖，以有利于贫民。
English: The government took out 20,000 koku of rice and sold it at a reduced price to benefit the poor.

古文：己卯，虎入长寿坊元载家庙，射生将周皓引弩毙之。
现代文：二十日，老虎跑入长寿坊元载的家庙，善于射杀生物的射生将周皓用弓箭射死了老虎。
English: On the 20th, the tiger ran into the home temple of Yuan Zang of Changshoufang. Zhou Yu, who was good at shooting creatures, shot the tiger with a bow and arrow.

古文：冬十月乙卯，以汝州刺史孟皞为京兆尹。
现代文：冬十月二十一日，以汝州刺史孟白皋为京兆尹。
English: On October 21st in winter, Meng Bailuan, the Prince of Ruzhou, was proclaimed as the Prince of Zhao Yin.

古文：十一月辛未，禁畿内弋猎。
现代文：十一月二日，禁止在京城附近地区打猎。
English: On the 7th day of the 11th month, shooting is prohibited in the territory of Beijing and its surrounding towns.

古文：乙亥，门下侍郎、同中书门下平章事、卫国公杜鸿渐卒。
现代文：十一日，门下侍郎、同中书门下平章事、卫国公杜鸿渐去世。
English: On the 11th day of the month, Du Hongyan, a junior chamberlain, a junior high school teacher, a junior high school student, a junior high school student, a junior high school student, a junior high school student, a junior high school student, a junior high school student, a junior high school student, a junior high school student, a junior high school student, a junior high school student, a junior high school student, a junior high school student, a junior high school student, a junior high school student, a junior high school student, a junior high school student, a senior high school student, and a senior high school student passed away.

古文：丙子以左仆射、冀国公裴冕同中书门下平章事，充东都留守、河南淮南淮西山南东道副元帅。
现代文：十二日，以左仆射、冀国公裴冕任同中书门下平章事，充任东都留守、河南、淮南、淮西、山南东道副元帅。
English: On the 12th, he was appointed as the Vice Marshal of the Eastern Capital, Henan Province, Huainan Province, Huaixi Province, and Shannan Province, with Zuoying Zhao and Jiji Guofei as his subordinates.

古文：十二月乙未，敕左右补阙、拾遗、内供奉员左右各置两员，余罢之。
现代文：十二月一日，皇上诏令左补阙、右补阙、左拾遗、右拾遗，内供奉员左右各置两员，其余都不设左右两员。
English: On the first day of December, the emperor issued an imperial edict to set up the left and right compiling posts, the left and right collecting relics, and the left and right collecting relics. There were two left and two right staff members for each of the staff members, and there were no left and right staff members for the rest.

古文：戊戌，裴冕卒。
现代文：四日，裴冕去世。
English: On the fourth day, Fei Guan died.

古文：辛酉，敕京兆府税宜分作两等，上等每亩税一斗，下等税六升，能耕垦荒地者税二升。
现代文：二十一日，皇上命令京兆府的税应分作两等，上等田每亩税一斗，下等田每亩税六升，能够垦荒耕种的田地每亩税二升。
English: On the twenty-first day of the month, the emperor ordered that the taxes of Jingzhao Prefecture should be divided into two classes. The upper-class fields should be taxed one bucket per mu, the lower-class fields should be taxed six liters per mu, and the fields that can be ploughed and cultivated should be taxed two liters per mu.

古文：五年春正月乙丑朔。
现代文：大历五年春正月一日是朔日。
English: The first day of the first month of spring in the fifth year of the lunar calendar is New Year's Day.

古文：辛卯，以陕州节度使皇甫温判凤翔尹，充凤翔、河陇节度使；凤翔节度使李抱玉判梁州事，充山南西道节度使。
现代文：二十七日，以陕州节度使皇甫温兼任职务较低的凤翔尹，并充任凤翔、河陇节度使；凤翔节度使李抱玉兼任职务较低的梁州事，并充任山南西道节度使。
English: On the 27th, on the occasion of the festival of Shaanxi Province, Emperor Fu Wen was assigned to the lesser post of Feng Xiang Yin, and served as the festival delegate of Fengxiang and Hebei Province; on the occasion of the festival of Fengxiang Province, Li Baoyu was assigned to the lesser post of Liangzhou Province, and served as the festival delegate of Shannan West Road.

古文：壬申，河南尹张延赏兼御史大夫，充东都留守。
现代文：二十八日，河南尹张延赏兼任御史大夫，充任东都留守。
English: On the 28th, Yin Zhang Yanbo from Henan Province was awarded the post of imperial historian and stayed in Dongdu.

古文：罢河南、淮西、山南东道副元帅，所管军隶东都留守。
现代文：撤销河南、淮西、淮南、山南东道副元帅，这些地方所管辖的军队隶属于东都留守。
English: The vice-marshals of Henan, Huaixi, Huainan and Shannan were revoked. The military forces under the jurisdiction of these places were subordinated to Dongdu.

古文：二月戊戌，李抱玉移镇，凤翔军仇，纵兵大掠，数日乃止。
现代文：二月五日，李抱玉移兵镇守銩稨，凤翔军忿怒，放纵军队大肆抢劫掠夺，抢了数天以后才停止。
English: On February 5th, Li Baoyu transferred his troops to guard the city of Handan. The Fengxiang troops were furious and allowed the troops to loot and plunder freely. The looting only stopped after several days.

古文：己亥。废仙州，以襄城、叶县隶汝州。
现代文：六日，废除仙州，以襄城、叶县隶属汝州。
English: On the 6th, Xianzhou was abolished, and Xiangcheng and Ye County were attached to Ruzhou.

古文：诏罢鱼朝恩观军容使。
现代文：皇上诏令罢免鱼朝恩的观军容使。
English: Emperor's edict dismisses Yucho En's envoy to observe the war.

古文：己巳，朝恩自缢而死。
现代文：三月十日，鱼朝恩自缢而死。
English: On March 10, Yucho En committed suicide.

古文：戊寅，诏定京兆府户税。
现代文：十五日，诏令确定京兆府户税。
English: On the 15th, the imperial edict confirmed that the Beijing-Shanghai prefectural household tax.

古文：思与百辟卿士，励精于理，俾国经王道，可举而行，各宜承式，以恭尔位。
现代文：夏天的税收，上等田亩每亩税六升，下等田每亩税四升。秋天的税，上等田每亩税五升，下等田每亩税三升。
English: In the summer, the tax is six liters per mu for higher-grade fields and four liters per mu for lower-grade fields. In the fall, the tax is five liters per mu for higher-grade fields and three liters per mu for lower-grade fields.

古文：诸州置屯亦宜停。
现代文：荒田开垦后的田地每亩税二升。
English: After the reclamation of wasteland, the field tax is up to two liters per mu.

古文：于是悉以度支之务委于宰相。
现代文：于是全部以度支之任务委托给宰相。
English: As a result, all tasks related to the budget were delegated to the Prime Minister.

古文：辛卯，以兵部侍郎贾至为京兆尹。
现代文：二十八日，以兵部侍郎贾至为京兆尹。
English: On the 28th, Jia Zhi, the attendant of the Ministry of Military Affairs, was appointed as Jing Zhaoyun.

古文：以京西兵马使李忠臣为凤翔尹，代皇甫温。温移镇陕州。
现代文：以京西兵马使李忠臣为凤翔尹，代替皇甫温；皇甫温移兵镇守陕州。
English: Li Zhongchen was appointed as Feng Xiangyin to replace Emperor Fuwen; Emperor Fuwen moved his troops to guard Shaanxi.

古文：夏四月庚子，湖南都团练使崔旰为其兵马使臧玠所杀，玠据潭州为乱，沣州刺史杨子琳、道州刺史裴虬、衡州刺史杨漳出军讨玠。
现代文：夏四月八日，湖南都团练使崔馞被他的兵马使臧所杀。
English: On the 8th day of the 4th month of the summer, Cui Yao, the commander of the Hunan Provincial Military Region, was killed by his soldiers.

古文：乙巳夜，岁星入轩辕。
现代文：十三日夜晚，岁星进入轩辕星座。
English: On the evening of the 13th day, the year star entered the constellation of Aries.

古文：丙午，复置先农、马祖坛，祀之。
现代文：十四日，重新设立先农坛和马祖坛，加以祭祀。
English: On the 14th, the Farmer's Altar and the Mazu Altar were re-established and dedicated.

古文：丁未，封幽州节度使硃希彩为高密郡王。
现代文：十五日，封幽州节度使朱希彩为高密郡王。
English: On the fifteenth day, the Fenyuzhou Festival made Zhu Xisai the king of Gaomi County.

古文：己未夜，彗起五车，长三丈。
现代文：二十七日，彗星从五车星座升起，长有三丈。
English: On the 27th, the comet rose from the constellation of the Five Chariots and grew three feet tall.

古文：庚申，宰臣太原尹王缙入朝。
现代文：二十八日，宰相太原尹王缙入朝。
English: On the 28th, Prime Minister Taiyuan Yin Wangjun entered the imperial court.

古文：五月辛未，刑部侍郎黎干为桂州刺史、桂管防御经略招讨观察等使。
现代文：五月九日，刑部侍郎黎干为桂州刺史、桂管防御使、经略使、招讨使、观察使。
English: On May 9, Li Gan, the attendant of the Criminal Investigation Department, was appointed as the Guizhou chief historian, the Guizhou defense envoy, the economic envoy, the solicitation envoy, and the observation envoy.

古文：己卯夜，彗起北方，其色白。
现代文：十七日夜，彗星起于北方，白颜色。
English: On the night of the 17th, the comet rose in the north, white in color.

古文：庚辰，贬礼仪使、礼部尚书裴士淹为虔州刺史，户部侍郎、判度支第五琦为饶州刺史。皆鱼朝恩党也。
现代文：十八日，贬礼仪使、礼部尚书裴士淹为虔州刺史，户部侍郎、兼任较低职务的度支使第五琦为饶州刺史，这是因为他们都是鱼朝恩的党羽。
English: On the 18th, the etiquette envoy, the etiquette department's Shang Shu Pei Ruan, was demoted to the status of Kenzhou's secretary, and the housekeeper of the household department, who also served as a lower-ranking official, the fifth-ranked official, was demoted to the status of Raozhou's secretary. This was because they were all party members of Yu Chaon.

古文：元载既诛朝恩，下制罢使，仍放黜之。
现代文：元载已经杀了鱼朝恩，下达皇帝的命令，罢免他们虔州刺史、礼仪使、饶州刺史等官职，仍旧放逐罢免了他们。
English: Yuan Zang had already killed Yu Chaon and issued the emperor's order to dismiss them from the posts of Qianzhou Jishi, Ceremonial Envoy, and Raozhou Jishi, and still banished and dismissed them.

古文：癸未，以羽林大将军辛京杲为潭州刺史、湖南观察使。
现代文：二十一日，以羽林大将军辛京杲为潭州刺史、湖南观察使。
English: On the twenty-first day of the month, Xin Jingyao, a general of the Yulin army, was appointed as the historian of Tanzhou and the observer of Hunan.

古文：甲申，西北白气竟天。
现代文：二十二日，西北方白气布满整个天空。
English: On the 22nd, white gas from the northwest filled the entire sky.

古文：徙置当、悉、柘、静、恭五州于山险要害地，备吐蕃也。
现代文：改移设置当、悉、柘、静、恭五州到山险要害之地，以防备吐蕃。
English: Five prefectures, including Dang, Siyi, Min, Jing and Gong, will be moved to the critical areas in order to prevent floods.

古文：六月己未彗星始灭，赦天下见禁囚徒。
现代文：六月二十八日，彗星开始熄灭，皇上赦免天下被关押的囚犯。
English: On June 28, the comet began to fade, and the emperor pardoned all prisoners.

古文：秋七月丁卯，以浙东观察使、越州刺史、御史大夫薛兼训为检校工部尚书、太原尹、北都留守，充河东节度使。
现代文：秋七月七日，以浙东观察使、越州刺史、御史大夫薛兼训为检校工部尚书、太原尹、北都留守，充任河东节度使。
English: On the 7th day of the 7th month of autumn, Shang Shu, Taiyuan Yin and Beidou from the inspection department of the school were left behind, with the East Zhejiang observation envoy, the Yuezhou chief historian and the chief historian Xue Jianxun, acting as the envoy of the festival in Hedong.

古文：是月，京城斗米千文。
现代文：这月，京城一斗大米一千文。
English: This month, a barrel of rice in Beijing costs 1,000 mon.

古文：八月辛卯，宰臣元载上疏请置中都于河中府，秋杪行幸，春中还京，以避蕃戎侵寇之患。
现代文：八月一日，宰相元载上奏疏请求把中都归到河中府，可以回避吐蕃入侵的祸患。上奏的疏章没有回音。
English: On August 1st, Prime Minister Yuan Zang requested that the capital be moved to Hechuan, so as to avoid the threat of invasion from Tibet. There was no response to his request.

古文：疏入不报。载疏大旨以关辅、河东等十州户税入奉京师，创置精兵五万，以威四方。辞多捭阖，欲权归于己也。
现代文：元载又上奏分析这大略旨要是因为京畿、河东等十州户税入奉到京师，可以创立五万精兵，以此威震四方，辞句多分化、拉拢之意，是想要大权归于自己。
English: In the Yuan Zhao, it was analyzed that if this grand plan was because the household taxes of ten states, such as Gyeonggi and Hedong, were sent to Beijing, it would be possible to create fifty thousand elite soldiers, so that they would be powerful in all directions. The meaning of the phrase "multiply" and "attract" is to want to have great power to oneself.

古文：九月丁丑，以宣、歙、池等州都团练观察使、宣州刺史、兼御史中丞陈少游充浙江东道团练观察使。
现代文：九月十八日，以宣、歙、池等州都团练观察使、宣州刺史、兼御史中丞陈少游充任浙江东道团练观察使。
English: On September 18th, with Xuan, Zou, Chi and other prefectures as the observation envoys for the group exercise, and Chen Shaoyou, the vice-president of Xuan, Zou and Zhou prefectures, as the host observation envoy for the group exercise in Zhejiang.

古文：吐蕃寇永寿。
现代文：吐蕃入侵永寿。
English: The invasion of the Tibetan mastiff into Yongshou.

古文：汴州田神功来朝。
现代文：汴州田神功前来朝见。
English: Zhangzhou Tian Shengong came to see the morning.

古文：十二月乙未，改巫州为溆州，业州为蒋州。
现代文：十二月七日，改巫州为溆州，业州为蒋州。
English: On December 7, Wuzhou was changed to Zhangzhou, and Yezhou to Jiangzhou.

古文：六年春正月己未朔。
现代文：大历六年春正月一日是朔日。
English: The first day of the first month of spring in the sixth year of the lunar calendar is New Year's Day.

古文：戊寅，于鄜州之鄜城置肃戎军。
现代文：二十日，在州之城设置肃戎军。
English: On the 20th, the Imperial Army was set up in Suzhou City.

古文：二月乙酉御史大夫敬括卒。
现代文：二月二十二日，御史大夫敬括去世。
English: On February 22nd, Dr. Mishi passed away.

古文：夏四月丁巳，上御宣政殿试制举人，至夕，策未成者，令太官给烛，俾尽其才。
现代文：夏四月一日，皇上驾到宣政殿考试应制举人。到晚上，策论尚没有写成者，皇上命令太官供给蜡烛，以便使他们各尽其才。
English: On the first day of the fourth month of the summer, the emperor arrived at the Xuancheng Palace to examine the candidates for the examination. By the evening, the policy had not yet been written, and the emperor ordered the eunuchs to provide candles so that they could do their best.

古文：五月癸卯，以河南尹张延赏为御史大夫。
现代文：三日，澧州刺史杨子琳前来朝见，皇上赐名为猷。二十一日，改果州为充州。五月十八日，以河南尹张延赏为御史大夫。
English: On the third day, Yang Zilin, the Empress Dowager of Zhangzhou, came to see the emperor, and the emperor gave her the title of Empress Dowager. On the 21st day, Guozhou was changed to Chengzhou. On May 18th, Yin Zhang Yan of Henan Province was awarded the title of Grand Historian.

古文：秋七月乙巳，月掩毕。
现代文：秋七月二十一日，月亮遮掩了毕星。
English: On the 21st day of the 7th month of autumn, the moon covered the stars.

古文：八月乙卯，淮南节度使韦元甫卒。
现代文：八月二日，淮南节度使韦元甫去世。
English: On August 2, Huainan Festival, Wei Yuanfu passed away.

古文：庚午，以御史大夫张延赏为扬州大都督府长史、淮南节度使。
现代文：三日，以东都副留守常休明为检校左散骑常侍、河阳三城使。
English: On the third day, Jokyu Ming, the deputy governor of Dongdu, left for the inspection of the school, and his attendants rode on horseback to the left, and the envoys from the three cities of Kayan came.

古文：丙午、以苏州刺史、浙江观察使李栖筠为御史大夫。
现代文：二十三日，以苏州刺史、浙江观察使李栖筠为御史大夫。
English: On the 23rd, with Suzhou chief historian and Zhejiang observation envoy Li Jiechi as chief historian.

古文：丁丑，获白兔于太极殿之内廊。
现代文：二十四日，在太极殿之内廊获得一只白兔。
English: On the 24th, a white rabbit was found in the inner corridor of the Taiji Hall.

古文：庚辰夜，月入紫微垣。
现代文：二十七日夜，月亮侵入紫微垣星座。
English: On the evening of the 27th, the moon entered the constellation of Violet Weak Wall.

古文：九月壬辰夜，荧惑犯哭星。
现代文：九月九日夜，荧惑星侵犯哭星。
English: On the night of September 9th, the crying star was invaded by a fluorescent planet.

古文：自八月连雨，害秋稼。
现代文：从八月以来，连续下雨，危害了庄稼。
English: Continuous rains since August have damaged crops.

古文：戊申，于轮台置静塞军。
现代文：二十五日，在轮台设置静塞军。
English: On the 25th, the garrison was set up at the wheelhouse.

古文：辛亥，荧惑入壁垒。冬十月壬午，沧州置横海军。
现代文：冬十月三十日，沧州设置横海军。
English: In the winter of October 30th, Cangzhou set up a horizontal navy.

古文：十一月己亥，文单国王婆弥来朝，献驯象一十一。
现代文：十一月十七日，文单国王婆弥前来朝见，贡献驯服好的大象十一头。
English: On November 17th, King Bhumibol Adulyadej came to see the emperor and donated eleven tame elephants.

古文：壬寅夜，月入太微，又掩氐。
现代文：二十日夜，月亮侵入太微星座，又遮掩了氐星。
English: On the night of the 20th, the moon entered the faint constellation and occulted the bright star.

古文：十二月己未，江西观察使、检校刑部尚书魏少游卒。
现代文：十二月七日，江西观察使、检校刑部尚书魏少游去世。
English: On December 7, Shangshu Wei Shaoyou, the Jiangxi observation envoy and head of the school inspection and punishment department, passed away.

古文：庚午，制以文单王婆弥开府仪同三司、试殿中监。
现代文：十八日，皇上下令以文单王婆弥为开府仪同三司，试用为殿中监。
English: On the 18th, the emperor ordered that Wenshan Wangbaya be appointed as the keeper of ceremonies and the third secretary, and he was put on probation as the palace middle supervisor.

古文：是岁春旱，米斛至万钱。
现代文：这年春天大旱灾，大米一斛达到一万钱。
English: In the spring of this year, there was a severe drought, and the price of a bushel of rice rose to ten thousand yuan.

古文：七年春正月癸未朔。
现代文：大历七年春正月一日是朔日。
English: The first day of the first month of spring in the seventh year of the lunar calendar is New Year's Day.

古文：戊子，于魏州顿邱县置澶州。
现代文：六日，在魏州顿丘县设置澶州。
English: On the 6th, in Dongqiu County, Weizhou, set up Zhangzhou.

古文：以顿邱县之观城店置观城县，以张之清丰店置清丰县，并割魏州之临黄县，并隶澶州。
现代文：以顿丘县之观城店设置观城县，以张县之清丰店设清丰县，并且分割魏州之临黄县，一起隶属澶州。
English: Set up Guancheng County with Guancheng Store in Dongqiu County, set up Qingfeng County with Qingfeng Store in Zhang County, and divided Linhuang County in Weizhou, all of which belong to Ganzhou.

古文：以贝州临清县之张桥店置永济县。
现代文：以贝州临清县之张桥店设置永济县。
English: The Zhangqiao store in Linqing County, Beizhou, was moved to Yongji County.

古文：乙未，月犯轩辕。
现代文：八日，月亮侵犯轩辕星座。
English: On the 8th, the moon will invade the constellation of Regulus.

古文：庚子，以检校户部尚书路嗣恭为洪州刺史、兼御史大夫、江西观察使。
现代文：十三日，以检校户部尚书路嗣恭为洪州刺史、兼御史大夫、江西观察使。
English: On the 13th, with the inspection of the school, the head of the household department, Shang Shul, Zhi Qiong, was appointed as the chief historian of Hongzhou, concurrently the chief historian, and the observation envoy of Jiangxi.

古文：辛丑，太常卿杨绾兼充礼仪使。
现代文：十四日，太常卿杨绾兼任礼仪使。
English: On the 14th, Yang Jie, the First Secretary of the Central Military Commission, also served as the ceremonial envoy.

古文：甲辰，回纥使出鸿胪寺劫坊市，吏不能禁止，复三百骑犯金光、硃雀等门。
现代文：十七日，回纥使者走出鸿胪寺抢劫掳掠市场，官吏不能禁止，又用三百骑兵侵犯金光、朱雀等门。
English: On the 17th, the emissaries of the Hui Dynasty came out of Hongye Temple to rob and plunder the market. The officials could not forbid them, and they also used three hundred cavalrymen to invade Jin Guang, Suzaku and other gates.

古文：是日皇城诸门皆闭，慰谕之方止。
现代文：这天皇城各门都关闭，安抚以后才停止侵扰。
English: All the gates of the emperor's castle were closed, and the intrusion only stopped after it was pacified.

古文：二月甲寅，以兵部侍郎李涵为苏州剌史、兼御史中丞，充浙西观察使。
现代文：二月三日，以兵部侍郎李涵为苏州刺史、兼御史中丞，充任浙西观察使。
English: On February 3, Li Han, the attendant of the Ministry of Military Affairs, was appointed as the Suzhou chief historian and vice-chancellor of history, and served as the western Zhejiang observation envoy.

古文：镇星临太微。
现代文：镇星临近太微星。
English: Zhenxing is close to Taimixing.

古文：戊午夜，月掩天关。
现代文：七日夜，月亮掩盖了天关星。
English: On the night of the seventh day, the moon covered the celestial body.

古文：三月壬辰，诏谏议大夫置四员为定。
现代文：三月十一日，诏令谏议大夫设置四员为定准。
English: On March 11th, the Emperor issued an edict ordering the Council of Doctors to set four members as the standard.

古文：可大赦天下，见禁囚徒，罪无轻重，一切释放。
现代文：夏四月四日，回纥王子李秉义去世，他是归国在宫廷宿卫赐予的中原名。五月五日，下冰雹，大风吹断了树。六日夜，月亮进入了太微星。
English: On the 4th day of the 4th month of the summer, Prince Li Bingyi of Hubei died. He was the original name given by the palace guards when he returned to China. On the 5th day of the 5th month, hailstorms and high winds broke trees. On the night of the 6th day, the moon entered Taimixing.

古文：癸亥，以检校礼部尚书蒋涣充东都留守。
现代文：十一日，把忻州的七位帝王的画像迁徙到太原府之紫极宫。以检校礼部尚书蒋涣充任京都留守。
English: On the 11th day of the month, the portraits of the seven emperors of Bozhou were moved to the Shiji Palace in Taiyuan Prefecture.

古文：六月庚戌，有司言日蚀，阴云不见。
现代文：六月一日是朔日，有关官员说有日蚀，阴云太多看不见。
English: The first day of June is New Year's Day. Officials say there will be a solar eclipse, but there are too many clouds to see it.

古文：丁丑，诏诫薄葬，不得造假花果及金手脱宝钿等物。
现代文：二十八日，皇上下诏告诫要薄葬，不得制造假花果以及金手和宝钿等物。
English: On the 28th, the emperor issued an imperial edict to exhort people to have a thin funeral, and not to make fake flowers and fruits, gold bracelets, treasure chests and other things.

古文：秋七月癸巳，回纥蕃客夺长安县令邵说所乘马，人吏不能禁。
现代文：秋七月十四日，回纥蕃人客商夺取长安县令邵说所乘之马，人们和官吏不能禁止。
English: On the 14th day of the 7th month of autumn, the Uighur merchants seized the horse of Chang'an County, and the people and officials could not stop them.

古文：八月庚戌，赐北庭都护曹令忠姓名曰李元忠。
现代文：八月二日，皇上赐北庭都护曹令忠姓名叫李元忠。
English: On August 2nd, the emperor bestowed the title of North Court Protector to Cao Lingzhong, whose name was Li Yuanzhong.

古文：九月乙未，工部尚书于休烈卒。
现代文：九月十七日，工部尚书于休烈去世。
English: On September 17th, Shang Shu of the Engineering Department passed away in Huling.

古文：冬十月壬子，上畋于苑中，矢一发贯二兔，从臣皆贺。
现代文：冬十月五日，皇上在御花园中打猎，一箭射穿了两只兔子，侍从之臣都祝贺。
English: On the 5th of October in winter, the emperor was hunting in the imperial garden. He shot an arrow through two rabbits, and his attendants congratulated him.

古文：辛未，以权知幽州卢龙节度留后硃泚检校左散骑常侍，充幽州卢龙节度使。
现代文：二十四日，以暂代幽州、卢龙节度留后朱氵此为检校左散骑常侍，充任幽州、卢龙节度使。
English: On the 24th, after staying in Yuzhou and Lulong for the temporary Yuzhou and Lulong festivals, Zhu Xi became the left rider of the school inspection, and served as the Yuzhou and Lulong festival envoy.

古文：丙子，以太府卿吕崇贲为广州都督，充岭南节度使。
现代文：二十九日，以太府卿吕崇贲为广州都督，充任岭南节度使。
English: On the 29th, Lv Chongyong, the governor of Yue Prefecture, became the governor of Guangzhou and served as the delegate to the Lingnan Festival.

古文：十一月庚辰，诏：自顷蕃戎入寇，巴南屡多征役。其巴、蓬、渠、集、壁、充、通、开等州，宜放二年租庸。
现代文：十一月四日，皇上下诏：自从近来吐蕃、回纥等蕃人军队入侵，巴南屡次征战，巴、蓬、渠、壁、充、通、开等州，应该免除两年赋税。
English: On November 4th, the emperor issued an imperial edict: Since the recent invasion of the Hunnic armies of Tubo and Hui, Banan has been repeatedly invaded, and the provinces of Ba, Peng, Qu, Wai, Chong, Tong, and Ka should be exempted from two years of taxation.

古文：甲申，以福建观察使李承昭为礼部尚书，华州刺史李琦为福州刺史、福建都团练观察使。
现代文：八日，以福建观察使李承昭为礼部尚书，华州刺史李琦为福州刺史、福州都团练观察使。
English: On the 8th, Li Chengzhao, the Fujian observation envoy, was appointed as the ceremonial secretary, and Li Wei, the Huazhou observation envoy, was appointed as the Fuzhou observation envoy and the Fuzhou capital group exercise observation envoy.

古文：辛卯，以岭南节度李勉为工部尚书。
现代文：十五日，以岭南节度使李勉为工部尚书。
English: On the 15th, with the Lingnan Festival, Li Qian was appointed as the Minister of Industry.

古文：十二月丙寅，雨士。
现代文：十二月二十日，下黄土。
English: December 20th, Lower Loess.

古文：是夜，长星出于参。
现代文：这一夜，长星从参星生出。
English: On this night, a star is born from a star.

古文：辛未，滑州置永平军。
现代文：二十五日，滑州设置永平军。
English: On the 25th, Yongping Army was set up in Nanzhou.

古文：壬子，禁铸铜器。
现代文：二十六日，禁止铸造铜器。
English: On the 26th, the casting of bronze ware was prohibited.

古文：癸酉，大雪。
现代文：二十七日，下大雪。
English: On the 27th, it snowed heavily.

古文：是秋稔。
现代文：这年秋天丰收。
English: This autumn was a bumper harvest.

古文：回纥、吐蕃、大食、渤海、室韦、靺鞨、契丹、奚、牂柯、康国、石国并遣使朝贡。
现代文：回纥、吐蕃、大食、渤海、室韦、革末革曷、契丹、奚、柯、康国、石国都派遣使者前来朝贡。
English: Huizhou, Tubo, Daxing, Bohai, Murowe, Qumuqin, Qidan, Yao, Ke, Kangguo and Shiguo all sent envoys to pay tribute.

古文：八年春正月丁丑朔，壬午，昭义军节度、检校右仆射、相州刺史薛嵩卒。
现代文：大历八年正月一日是朔日。六日，昭义军节度、检校右仆射、相州刺史薛嵩去世。
English: The first day of the first month of the eighth year of the lunar calendar is the new moon day. On the sixth day, the Shouyi Army Festival, the inspection of the school, and the death of Xue Song.

古文：癸卯，敕天下青苗地头钱每亩十五文，率京畿三十文，自今一例十五文。
现代文：二十七日，皇上命令天下青苗地头钱每亩交十五文，京城附近原先是每亩三十文，从今起一律都交十五文。
English: On the 27th, the emperor ordered the young seedlings in the world to pay 15 mon per mu of land, and the area near the capital was originally 30 mon per mu. From now on, they will all pay 15 mon.

古文：京官三品已上郎官御史，每年各举一人堪为刺史县令者。
现代文：京官三品以上郎官、御史，每年各举一人完全能胜任刺史县令的人。
English: Every year, one person who is fully capable of serving as the county magistrate of Shishi will be appointed to the post of lokan and goshi above the rank of kyokan sanbon.

古文：二月甲子，御史大夫李栖筠弹吏部侍郎徐浩。
现代文：二月十九日，御史大夫李栖筠弹劾吏部侍郎徐浩。
English: On February 19th, the chief historian, Li Qisheng, impeached Xu Hao, the secretary of the cadre department.

古文：丁卯，幽州节度使硃泚加检校户部尚书，封怀宁郡王。
现代文：二十二日，赐给幽州节度使朱氵此检校户部尚书的加官，封为怀宁郡王。
English: On the 22nd, the Yuzhou Festival gave Zhu Xi the additional post of inspecting the school's household department, and he was named the king of Huaining County.

古文：徐浩、薛邕违格，并停知选事。
现代文：徐浩、薛邕违法，都停止主持选拔官员之事。
English: Xu Hao and Xue Yao both violated the law and ceased to preside over the selection of officials.

古文：壬申，永平军节度使、检校右仆射、滑州刺史、霍国公令狐彰卒，遣表荐刘晏、李勉代己。
现代文：二十七日，永平军节度使、检校右仆射、滑州刺史、霍国公令狐彰去世，遗留下的表章推荐刘晏、李勉代替自己。
English: On the 27th, the Yongping Army's commander-in-chief, the inspector-in-chief, the right-hand man, the inspector-in-chief, the inspector-in-chief of Leshou, the inspector-in-chief of Huo, and the official of Huo, the official of the State Council, the official of the State Council, the official of the State Council, the official of the State Council of the People's Republic of China, the official of the State Council of the People's Republic of China, the official of the State Council of the People's Republic of China, the official of the State Council of the People's Republic of

古文：三月丙子，以工部尚书李勉兼御史大夫、滑州刺史，充永平军节度、滑亳观察等使。
现代文：三月一日，以工部尚书李勉兼御史大夫、滑州刺史，并充任永平军节度使、滑州、亳州观察使。
English: On March 1st, he was appointed as Shangshu Li Tsun of the Ministry of Industry and Mines, as well as the chief historian and the historian of Nanzhou, and served as the Yongping Army's festival envoy, and the observation envoy of Nanzhou and Zhangzhou.

古文：夏四月戊申，乾陵上仙观天尊殿有双鹊衔紫泥补殿之隙缺，凡十五处。
现代文：夏四月三日，乾陵上仙观、天尊殿有一双喜鹊口衔紫泥弥补宫陵殿上的缝隙缺损，总计补了十五处。
English: On the 3rd day of the 4th month of the summer, there was a pair of magpie mouth-shaped purple mud to make up for the gaps on the Qianling Mausoleum, and a total of fifteen places were made up.

古文：戊午，以太仆卿吴仲孺为鄂州刺史、鄂岳沔等州团练观察使。
现代文：十三日，以太仆卿吴仲孺为鄂州刺史、鄂州、岳州、沔州的团练使、观察使。
English: On the 13th, Ether Servant Wu Zhongya was appointed as the group training envoy and observation envoy for the Ezhou Sashih, Ezhou, Yuezhou and Zhangzhou.

古文：五月乙酉，贬吏部侍郎徐浩明州别驾，薛邕歙州刺史，京兆尹杜济杭州刺史，皆坐典选也。
现代文：五月十一日，贬吏部侍郎徐浩为明州别驾，薛邕为歙州刺史，京兆尹杜济为杭州刺史，他们都犯了错选官员的罪。
English: On May 11th, Xu Hao, the secretary of the Department of Censors, was appointed as the governor of Mingzhou, Xue Yao was appointed as the governor of Zhangzhou, and Jing Zhaoyin Duji was appointed as the governor of Hangzhou. They all committed the crime of wrongly electing officials.

古文：以太府卿于颀为京兆尹。
现代文：以太府卿于颀为京兆尹。
English: With the Taifu-kyo Yu Shun as the leader, he became known as Keizhoin.

古文：辛卯，郑王邈薨，赠昭静太子。
现代文：十七日，郑王邈去世，赠为昭静太子。
English: On the 17th, Zheng Wangtao passed away and was presented to Prince Zhao Jing.

古文：壬辰，曲赦京城系囚。
现代文：十八日，特别赦免京城中被关押的囚犯。
English: On the 18th, a special amnesty was granted to prisoners held in Kyoto.

古文：癸卯，诏赦天下系囚，死罪降从流，流已下并放。
现代文：二十九日，皇上诏令赦免天下被关押的囚犯，死罪减轻为流放，流放以下的罪人都释放。
English: On the 29th, the emperor issued a decree to pardon all the prisoners in the world. The death penalty was reduced to banishment, and all the criminals below banishment were released.

古文：六月陇州华亭县置义宁军。
现代文：六月，陇州华亭县设置义宁军。
English: In June, the Yining Army was set up in Huating County, Zhangzhou.

古文：癸亥，户部侍郎、判度支韩滉奏安邑盐池生乳盐。
现代文：十九日，户部侍郎、兼任度支使韩上奏说安邑盐池产出了乳盐。
English: On the 19th, Han Sang-soo, the chief steward of the household and concurrently the chief of staff, reported that milk salt had been produced in the salt ponds of Ami.

古文：是夏，城奉天以备蕃寇。
现代文：这年夏天，在奉天筑城墙以防备蕃人入侵。
English: In the summer of this year, the city wall was built in Bongtian to prevent the invasion of the Xiongnu.

古文：秋七月己卯，太白入东井。
现代文：秋七月六日，太白星进入东井。
English: On the 6th day of the 7th month of autumn, Taibai Xing entered the East Well.

古文：乙未，月掩毕。
现代文：二十二日，月亮遮掩了毕星。
English: On the 22nd, the moon eclipsed the star.

古文：八月甲寅，诏吏部尚书刘晏知三铨选事。
现代文：八月十一日，皇上诏令吏部尚书刘晏主持考核选拔官员事。
English: On August 11th, the emperor issued an imperial edict ordering the librarian, Shangshu Liu Wei, to preside over the examination and selection of officials.

古文：己未，吐蕃寇灵武。
现代文：十六日，吐蕃入侵灵武。
English: On the 16th, the Tuoba invaded Lingwu.

古文：庚午，灵武奏蕃军退去。
现代文：二十七日，灵武地方上奏吐蕃侵略军退走。
English: On the 27th, the invading troops withdrew from Lingwu.

古文：辛未，幽州节度使硃泚弟滔率五千骑来朝，请河西防秋。
现代文：二十八日，幽州节度使朱氵此弟朱滔率领五千骑兵前来朝见，请求到河西秋防。
English: On the 28th, the Yuzhou Festival made Zhu Yao's younger brother Zhu Tao lead five thousand cavalry to come to see the emperor and request to go to the autumn defense in Hexi.

古文：诏千骑迓于国门，许自皇城南面出开远门，赴泾州行营。
现代文：诏令一千骑兵在国门迎接。同意他们从皇城南面出开远门，奔赴泾州行营。
English: The emperor ordered a thousand cavalry to meet them at the gate of the country, and agreed that they should leave the southern part of the imperial city and go to the camp in Zhangzhou.

古文：九月癸酉，临晋公主薨。
现代文：九月一日，临晋公主去世。
English: On September 1, Princess Linjin passed away.

古文：壬午，岭南节度使、广州刺史吕崇贲为部将哥舒晃所杀。
现代文：十日，岭南节度使、广州刺史吕崇贲被部将哥舒晃所杀。
English: On the 10th day of the month, the Lingnan Festival envoy, the Guangzhou chief of staff, Lv Chongyong, was killed by the general of the department, Goshukang.

古文：癸未，晋州男子郇谟以麻辫发，持竹筐及苇席，哭于东市，请进三十字，如不称旨，请裹尸于席筐。
现代文：十一日，晋州男子郇谟以麻系住头上发辫，拿着竹筐和苇席，在东市哭，请求向皇上进献三十个字，如果不符合皇上旨意，请求自杀将尸体裹在竹筐苇席中。
English: On the 11th day of the month, Jinzhou man Zou Meng tied a hairpin around his head with a hemp cord, took a bamboo basket and a feast, cried in Dongshi, asked to present 30 words to the emperor, and if it did not meet the emperor's will, asked to commit suicide by wrapping the body in a bamboo basket and a feast.

古文：上召见，赐衣馆之禁中。
现代文：皇上召见，赐给衣服，在宫中给他一馆住下。
English: The emperor summoned him, gave him clothes, and gave him a palace to live in.

古文：内二字曰 监团 ，欲去诸道监军、团练使也。
现代文：皇上采纳了二字曰 监团 ，想免除各道监军和团练使。
English: The emperor adopted the two words "supervisory group" in order to exempt the supervisors of each province and the group training envoys.

古文：丁亥，贬左巡使、殿中侍御史杨护，以其抑郇谟而不上闻也，戊子，诏京官五品以上各上封事，议政得失。
现代文：十五日，贬左巡使、殿中侍御史杨护，因为他压抑郇谟而不使皇上听闻。十六日，诏令京官五品以上官员各上密封的章奏，谈论政事得失。
English: On the 15th, the left-wing envoy and palace attendant Shi Yangfu was demoted, because he suppressed the rumor and did not let the emperor hear it. On the 16th, the imperial edict ordered the officials of the Beijing government above the fifth grade to each play a sealed chapter and discuss the gains and losses of political affairs.

古文：己丑夜，太白入太微。
现代文：十七日夜，太白星进入太微星座。
English: On the evening of the 17th, the Taibai Star entered the Taibai constellation.

古文：甲午，东都留守蒋琼兼知东都贡举。
现代文：二十二日，东都留守蒋琼兼任主持东都科举考试。
English: On the 22nd, Jiang Qiong stayed in Dongdu to preside over the Dongdu Science Examination.

古文：戊戌，以辰、锦观察使李昌巙为桂州刺史、桂管防御观察使。
现代文：二十六日，以辰、锦观察使李昌为桂州刺史、桂管防御观察使。
English: On the 26th, with the observation of Chen and Jin, Li Chang was appointed as the Guizhou history and Guizhou defense observation envoy.

古文：大鸟见武功，肉翅狐首，四足有爪，爪长四尺三寸，毛赤如蝙蝠，群鸟随而噪之。
现代文：有一只大鸟在武功出现，肉翅膀，狐狸的头，四只脚有爪子，爪长四尺三寸，毛赤红色如蝙蝠，群鸟随着它鸣叫。
English: A large bird appeared in the martial arts. It had fleshy wings, the head of a fox, and four clawed feet. The claws were four feet and three inches long. Its fur was red and red like a bat. The birds chirped along with it.

古文：神策将张日芬射毙以献。
现代文：神策将张日芬将它射死献给皇上。
English: Shinsaku had Zhang Rifen shoot it dead and present it to the emperor.

古文：冬十月癸卯，魏博田承嗣加同平章事。
现代文：冬十月一日，魏博田承嗣加任同平章事。
English: On the first day of October in winter, Wei Botian Shouji was appointed to the position of Tongping Zhangji.

古文：丁巳夜，月掩毕。
现代文：十五日夜，月亮遮掩了毕星。
English: On the evening of the fifteenth day, the moon covered the stars.

古文：吐蕃寇泾州、邠州。
现代文：吐蕃入侵泾州、州。
English: The pigeons have invaded Zhangzhou and Zhouzhou.

古文：甲子，子仪先锋将珲瑊与吐蕃战于宜录，我师不利。
现代文：二十二日，郭子仪的先锋将浑王咸在宜禄与吐蕃作战，我军不利。
English: On the 22nd, Guo Ziyi's vanguard sent Hun Wang Xian to fight against Tubo in Yilu. Our army was at a disadvantage.

古文：瑊与泾原马璘极力追蹑，蕃军溃去。
现代文：浑王咸与泾原马瞞极力跟踪追赶，吐蕃军溃退而去。
English: Hun Wangxian and Qianyuan Ma Xie tried their best to follow and catch up, but the Tubo army broke and retreated.

古文：乙丑，以江西观察使路嗣恭为广州刺史，充岭南节度使，封翼国公。
现代文：二十三日，以江西观察使路嗣恭为广州刺史，并充任岭南节度使，封翼国公。
English: On the 23rd, Jiangxi observation envoy Lu Shigong made history in Guangzhou, and served as the Lingnan festival envoy, sealing the wings of the country.

古文：以浙东观察使、越州刺史陈少游为扬州大都督府长史，充淮南节度使。
现代文：以浙东观察使、越州刺史陈少游为扬州大都督府长史，充任淮南节度使。
English: Chen Shaoyou, the observer of East Zhejiang and the chief historian of Yuezhou, was appointed as the governor of Yangzhou and the chief historian of Huainan.

古文：戊辰，郭子仪奏破吐蕃十万，百僚称贺。
现代文：二十六日，郭子仪上奏攻破吐蕃十万兵，百官向皇上祝贺。
English: On the twenty-sixth day, Guo Ziyi made a speech about defeating 100,000 soldiers of Tu Wei, and hundreds of officials congratulated the emperor.

古文：己卯夜，月入羽林。
现代文：二十七日夜，月亮进入羽林星座。
English: On the evening of the 27th, the moon entered the constellation of the Feathered Forest.

古文：癸巳，月入太微。
现代文：三十日，月亮进入太微星座。
English: On the 30th, the moon entered the Taimu constellation.

古文：十一月壬寅朔。
现代文：十一月一日是朔日。
English: The first day of the first month of November is Jinsin Day.

古文：庚戌，汴宋节度使田神功来朝。
现代文：九日，汴宋节度使田神功前来朝见。
English: On the 9th, the Song Dynasty festival made Tian Shengong come to see the emperor.

古文：辛酉，淮西节度使李忠臣来朝。
现代文：二十日，淮西节度使李忠臣前来朝见。
English: On the 20th, the Huaxi Festival made Li Zhongchen come to see the emperor.

古文：十二月癸酉，月入羽林。
现代文：十二月三日，月亮进入羽林星座。
English: On December 3rd, the moon will enter the constellation of Aquila.

古文：是冬无雪。
现代文：这年冬天无雪。
English: There was no snow this winter.

古文：是岁大有年。
现代文：这年是丰收年。
English: This year is a bumper year.

古文：九年正月庚子朔。
现代文：大历九年春正月一日是朔日。
English: The first day of the first month of spring in the ninth year of the lunar calendar is the new year's day.

古文：壬寅，汴宋节度使、太子少师、检校尚书右仆射、兼御史大夫、汴州刺史田神功卒。
现代文：三日，汴宋节度使、太子少师、检校尚书右仆射、兼御史大夫、汴州刺史田神功去世。
English: On the third day of the month, Sheng Tian Shengong, an envoy of the Song and Song Dynasty, a young teacher of the prince, a school inspector, a scholar, and a historian, passed away.

古文：沣朗两州镇遏使、沣州刺史杨猷擅浮江而下，至鄂州。
现代文：澧、朗两州镇遏使、澧州刺史杨猷擅自浮江而下，到了鄂州。
English: The towns of the two prefectures of Handan and Lang, and the prefectural governor of Handan, Yang Jie, went down the Floating River without permission and arrived in Ezhou.

古文：诏许赴汝州，遂溯汉而上，复、郢、襄等州皆闭城拒之。
现代文：皇上诏令让他奔赴汝州，于是杨猷逆汉江而上，复、郢、襄等州都关闭城门抗拒他，不让他进城。
English: The emperor's edict ordered him to rush to Ruzhou, so Yang Xuan sailed up the Han River, and Fuzhou, Handan and Xiangzhou all closed their gates to resist him and not let him enter the city.

古文：二月己丑，以田神功弟神玉权知汴宋留后。
现代文：二月二十日，以田神功之弟田神玉暂代汴宋留后。
English: On February 20th, Tian Shengyu, the younger brother of Yida Shengong, became the temporary successor of Song.

古文：癸巳，郭子仪自邠州来朝，李抱玉自凤翔来朝。
现代文：二十四日，郭子仪从州前来朝见，李抱玉从凤翔前来朝见。
English: On the twenty-fourth day, Guo Ziyi came from the state to see the morning, and Li Baoyu came from Fengxiang to see the morning.

古文：三月丙午，禁畿内渔猎采捕，自正月至五月晦，永为常式。
现代文：三月七日，禁止在京城附近捕猎野兽打鱼，从正月到五月底，永远成为常规。
English: On March 7, the hunting of wild animals and fishing in the vicinity of the capital were banned, and from the first month to the end of May, it will always be the norm.

古文：戊子，以沣州刺史杨猷为洮州刺史。
现代文：十九日，以澧州刺史杨猷为洮州刺史。
English: On the 19th, Yang Jie, the governor of Zhangzhou, was named governor of Zhangzhou.

古文：夏四月丁丑，月入太微。
现代文：夏四月九日，月亮进入太微星座。
English: On the 9th day of the 4th month of the summer, the moon entered the Taimu constellation.

古文：己卯，以桂管观察使黎干为京兆尹、兼御史大夫。
现代文：十一日，以桂管观察使黎干为京兆尹、兼御史大夫。
English: On the 11th day of the month, Li Gan was appointed as the Keizhao Yin and the Imperial Historian.

古文：甲申，中书舍人常衮率两省官一十八人诣阁请论事，诏三人各尽所怀。
现代文：十六日，中书舍人常衮率领中书省门下省两省官员十八人到内阁请求论述朝事，皇上诏令三人各人尽量抒发个人的怀抱。
English: On the 16th, 18 officials from the two provinces under the leadership of the CLS, led by the CLS's deputy, Chang Qi, went to the cabinet to request a discussion of the situation in Korea. The emperor ordered the three officials to express their personal feelings as much as possible.

古文：乙酉，诏郭子仪等大阅兵师以备吐蕃。
现代文：十七日，诏令郭子仪等大阅兵以防备吐蕃。
English: On the 17th, he ordered Guo Ziyi and others to hold a large military parade to prevent the outbreak of war.

古文：壬辰，诏赦大辟以下系囚，无轻重释放。
现代文：二十四日，皇上诏令赦免死刑以下被关押的罪犯，无论轻重都释放。
English: On the 24th, the emperor issued an imperial edict to pardon prisoners sentenced to death or less, releasing them regardless of their severity.

古文：乙未，华阳公主薨，上悲惜之，累日不听朝，宰臣抗疏陈请。
现代文：二十七日，华阳公主去世，皇上悲痛怜惜她，几天不听朝，宰辅大臣上书劝谏请求皇上上朝。
English: On the 27th, Princess Huayang passed away. The Emperor grieved and pitied her. He did not listen to the Imperial Court for several days. The Vice-Minister of the Imperial Court sent a letter to the Emperor asking him to come to the Imperial Court.

古文：五月庚戌，废泜州。
现代文：五月十二日，撤销氵氐州。
English: On May 12, Zhangzhou was revoked.

古文：庚申，诏度支使支七十万贯、转运使五十万贯和籴，岁丰谷贱也。
现代文：二十二日，皇上诏令度支使支钱七十万贯、转运使支五十万贯来购买人民粮食，因为年成丰收谷物太便宜了。
English: On the 22nd, the emperor issued an imperial edict to spend 700,000 kroner for transportation and 500,000 kroner for transshipment to purchase grain for the people, because the annual bumper harvest of grain was too cheap.

古文：乙丑，诏：四海之内，方协大宁，西戎无厌，独阻王命，不可忘战，尚劳边事。
现代文：二十七日，皇上诏曰： 四海之内，四方诣和，非常安宁，西戎却不满足，独独抗拒王命，我们不可忘记战争，还要勤于防备边境战事。
English: On the 27th, the emperor issued an edict saying: "Within the four seas, peace has been made on all sides, and it is very peaceful. However, the West is not satisfied, and it alone resists the king's order. We must not forget the war, and we must also diligently prepare for border wars.

古文：朕顷以兵革之后，军国空耗，躬率节俭，务勤农桑。上玄储休，仍岁大稔，益用多愧，不知其然。
现代文：朕因为近来战争之后，军队、国家勤劳于农桑。上天等待和平，连年丰收，越发使人深感惭愧，不知道上天为什么这样。
English: Because recently, after the war, the army and the country have been working hard on the farm. Heaven is waiting for peace, and the harvest has been plentiful for years. It makes people feel more and more ashamed. I don't know why Heaven is like this.

古文：虽属此人和，近于家给，而边谷未实，戎备犹虚。
现代文：虽然现在属于人民和谐之时，接近于家给人足，然而边境谷粮还不充实，军备还很空虚。
English: Though this is a time of harmony for the people, and sufficiency close to home, yet the borders are barren of grain and empty of arms.

古文：因其天时，思致丰积，将设平籴，以之餽军。
现代文：朕要依靠天时之利，想到丰收而积存粮食，将设立平价采购，以此送给军队作为军粮。
English: We should rely on the benefit of time, think of the bumper harvest and accumulate grain, will set up a parity purchase, in order to send to the army as military grain.

古文：然以中都所供，内府不足，粗充常入之数，岂齐倍余之收。
现代文：然而由于中都所供应，朝廷储备不充足，粗略地充当常规收入的数字，难道能够和加倍多余的收入齐平。
English: However, due to the fact that it is supplied by the central government, the imperial reserve is not sufficient, and the figure that roughly serves as regular income can only be equal to the double surplus income.

古文：其在方面荩臣，成兹大计。共佐公家之急，以资塞下之储。
现代文：那些在各地忠诚的大臣，应该成就这些国家大计，共同帮助解决国家的急难，以此来资助边疆粮食的储备。
English: Those ministers who are loyal in various regions should accomplish these national plans and jointly help solve the country's urgent problems, so as to fund the frontier grain reserves.

古文：每道岁有防秋兵马，其淮南四千人，浙西三千人，魏博四千人，昭义二千人，成德三千人，山南东道三千人，荆南二千人，湖南三千人，山南西道二千人，剑南西川三千人，东川二千人，鄂岳一千五百人。宣歙三千人，福建一千五百人。其岭南、浙东、浙西，亦合准例。
现代文：每个道每年有秋天防务的兵马，淮南四千人，浙西三千人，魏博四千人、昭义二千人，成德三千人，山南东道三千人，荆南二千人，湖南三千人，山南西道二千人，剑南西川三千人，东川二千人，鄂岳一千五百人，宣歙三千人，福建一千五百人，其余岭南、浙东、浙西，也应符合上述地方的例子为标准。
English: Each province has 4,000 soldiers for autumn defense every year, including 4,000 from Huainan Province, 3,000 from West Zhejiang Province, 4,000 from Weibo Province, 2,000 from Zhao Yi Province, 3,000 from Chengde Province, 3,000 from Shannan Host Province, 2,000 from Jingnan Province, 3,000 from Hunan Province, 2,000 from West Shannan Province, 3,000 from West Jianan Province, 2,000 from East Sichuan Province, 1,500 from Hougou Province, 3,000 from Xuanfan Province, and 1,500 from Fujian Province. The remaining soldiers from Lingnan Province, East Zhejiang Province, and West Zhejiang Province should also meet the above-mentioned standards.

古文：恐路远往来增费，各委本道每年取当使诸色杂钱及回易利润、赃赎钱等，每人计二十贯。
现代文：恐怕路远往来增加费用，各委托本道每年应当使用各色杂例钱和交易买卖的利润以及贪赃受贿的罪人的赎罪钱等等，每人合计二十贯。
English: I am afraid that the long-distance travel will increase the cost, and each trustee should annually use all kinds of miscellaneous money and the profits of trading and buying and selling, as well as the atonement money of the corrupt and bribe-taking criminals, etc., for a total of twenty yuan per person.

古文：每道据合配防秋人数多少，都计钱数，市轻货送纳上都，以备和籴，仍以秋收送毕。
现代文：每道依据配合秋防人数的多少，总计钱数，购买较轻的货物缴纳到上都，以准备购买粮食，供给军用，仍然在秋收时送完。 
English: Each way is based on the number of people participating in the autumn defense, the total amount of money, the purchase of lighter goods paid to Shangdu to prepare for the purchase of grain and supply to the military, and still sent at the autumn harvest.

古文：泾原节度使马璘来朝。
现代文：泾原节度使马瞞前来朝见。
English: The Empress Dowager Empress Dowager Empress Dowager Empress Dowager Empress Dowager Empress Dowager Empress Dowager

古文：丙寅，加马璘尚书左仆射、知省事。
现代文：二十八日，赐予马瞞尚书左仆射、主持尚书省事的职衔。
English: On the 28th, Ma Shide was given the title of the left-hand man of Shangshu, presiding over the affairs of Shangshu.

古文：璘讽将士进状求宰相，故有是授。
现代文：这是由于马瞞暗示将士进上陈述的文件请求做宰相，所以有这样的授予。
English: This was because Machethi had hinted that he wanted him to be the prime minister in the document he had submitted.

古文：幽州节度使硃泚遣弟滔奉表请自入朝，兼自率五千骑防秋。
现代文：幽州节度使朱氵此派遣弟弟朱滔奉上表章，请求自己入朝，并且亲自率领五千骑兵作为秋防。
English: The Yuzhou Festival made Zhu Xi send his younger brother Zhu Tao to present the badge, ask him to enter the imperial court, and personally lead five thousand cavalry as the autumn defense.

古文：许之，诏所司筑第待之。
现代文：皇上同意，诏有关部门建筑住宅以等待他。
English: The emperor agreed and ordered the relevant departments to build a residence to wait for him.

古文：六月己卯，月掩南斗。
现代文：六月十一日，月亮遮掩了南斗星。
English: On June 11, the moon eclipsed the Southern Dipper.

古文：庚辰，月入太微。
现代文：十二日，月亮进入太微星座。
English: On the 12th, the moon entered the faint constellation.

古文：秋七月甲辰，月掩房，又入羽林。久旱，京兆尹黎干历祷诸祠，未雨。
现代文：秋七月七日，月亮遮掩了房星，又进入羽林星座，长久干旱，京兆尹黎干到各类祠堂祈祷，没有下雨。
English: On the 7th day of the 7th month of autumn, the moon covered the house star and entered the constellation of the feather forest. There was a long drought, and Jing Zhao Yin Li went to various ancestral halls to pray. There was no rain.

古文：又请祷文宣庙，上曰 丘之祷久矣。 
现代文：又请求在文宣庙祈祷，皇上道： 孔丘祈祷已经很久了！ 
English: He also asked to pray at the Wen Xuan Temple. The emperor said, "It's been a long time since Confucius prayed!

古文：八月辛未，以虢州刺史宋晦为同州刺史，充长春宫营田等使。
现代文：八月四日，以虢州刺史宋晦为同州刺史，并充任长春宫营田使。
English: On August 4th, Song Gui, the governor of Zhangzhou, was appointed as the governor of Zhangzhou, and also served as the field marshal of the Changchun Palace.

古文：戊寅，以陕州大都督府长史皇甫温为越州剌史，充浙东观察使。
现代文：十一日，以陕州大都督府长史皇甫温为越州刺史，充任浙东观察使。
English: On the 11th, the governor of the great capital of Shaanxi Province, Shi Huangfuwen, was appointed as the ambassador of Yuezhou and the observer of East Zhejiang.

古文：辛卯，月掩轩辕。
现代文：二十四日，月亮遮掩了轩辕星座。
English: On the 24th, the moon obscured the constellation of Virgo.

古文：九月庚子，幽州节度使硃泚来朝。
现代文：九月四日，幽州节度使朱氵此前来朝见。
English: On September 4, the Yuzhou Festival made Zhu Xi come to see the emperor.

古文：乙巳，渭北节度使、坊州刺史臧希让卒。
现代文：九日，渭北节度使、坊州刺史臧希让去世。
English: On the 9th, the chief envoy of the Northern Song Dynasty and the chief envoy of the Southern Song Dynasty died.

古文：是秋大雨。
现代文：这年秋天下大雨。
English: It rained heavily in the autumn of that year.

古文：冬十月壬申，信王瑝薨。
现代文：冬十月六日，信王王皇去世。
English: On the 6th of October in winter, Emperor Shinno passed away.

古文：乙亥，梁王璿薨。
现代文：九日，梁王去世。
English: On the 9th, Liang Wang passed away.

古文：以前宣州刺史季广琛为右散骑常侍。
现代文：以前任宣州刺史季广琛为右散骑常侍。
English: Former Xuanzhou magistrate Ji Guangyao was the right rider.

古文：十一月戊戌，大雪。平地盈尺。
现代文：十一月三日，下大雪，平地雪满满一尺。
English: On November 3rd, heavy snow fell, and the flat ground was covered with a foot of snow.

古文：庚子，以商州刺史李国清为陕州大都督府长史，充陕州观察使。
现代文：五日，以商州刺史李国清为陕州大都督府长史，并充任陕州观察使。
English: On the 5th, Li Guoqing, the chief historian of Shangzhou, was appointed as the governor of Shaanxi, and served as the Shaanxi observation envoy.

古文：十二月庚寅，以中书舍人杨炎、秘书少监韦肇并为吏部侍郎，中书舍人常衮为礼部待郎。
现代文：十二月二十五日，以中书舍人杨炎、秘书少监韦肇都任吏部侍郎，中书舍人常衮任礼部侍郎。
English: On December 25th, Yang Yan, a junior high school teacher, and Wei Zhaodu, a junior high school secretary, were appointed as the attendants of the cadre department, and the junior high school teacher, Jang Hao, was appointed as the attendant of the ceremony department.

古文：壬辰，赦京系囚，死罪降从流，流已下并释放。
现代文：二十七日，赦免京师被关押的囚犯，死罪降低为流放，流放以下罪人都全部释放。
English: On the 27th, the prisoners held by the Beijing Division were pardoned, the death penalty was reduced to banishment, and all the criminals below banishment were released.

古文：十年春正月乙未朔。
现代文：大历十年春正月一日是朔日。
English: The first day of the first month of spring in the tenth year of the lunar calendar is the new moon.

古文：己酉，昭义牙将裴志清逐其帅薛摐，薛摐奔洺州，上章待罪。
现代文：十五日，昭义牙将裴志清驱逐他的大帅薛逃到了州，上奏章等待皇上判罪。
English: On the fifteenth day, Zhao Yiga expelled Pei Zhiqing and his general Xue fled to the state, awaiting the emperor's sentence.

古文：志清率众归田承嗣。
现代文：裴志清率众军归附了田承嗣。
English: Pei Zhiqing led the troops and annexed Tian Cheng He.

古文：壬寅，寿王瑁薨。
现代文：八日，寿王李瑁去世。
English: On the eighth day of the first month, the birthday king, Li Xi, passed away.

古文：乙未，硃泚抗表乞留京师，西征吐蕃，请以弟滔权为幽州留后，许之。
现代文：十一日，朱氵此极力上表请求离开京师，往西去攻打吐蕃，请求以弟弟朱滔暂代幽州留后，皇上同意了。
English: On the 11th day of the month, Zhu Xi made a strong request to leave the capital division and go west to attack Tujia. After requesting that his brother Zhu Tao temporarily stay in Yuzhou, the emperor agreed.

古文：以昭义将薛择为相州刺史，薛雄为卫州刺史，薛坚为洺州刺史，皆嵩之族人也。
现代文：以昭义的部将薛择为相州刺史，薛雄为卫州刺史，薛坚为州刺史，他们都是薛的族人。
English: Zhao Yi's general, Xue, was chosen as the chief historian of Xiangzhou, Xue Xiong as the chief historian of Weizhou, and Xue Jian as the chief historian of Xuzhou. They were all Xue's people.

古文：戊申，遣使慰谕田承嗣，令各守封疆，承嗣不奉诏。
现代文：十四日，皇上派遣使者安抚田承嗣，命令他们各人守护好封疆，而田承嗣不接受诏令。
English: On the 14th, the emperor sent an envoy to appease Tian Heung Hee, ordering each of them to guard the sealed territory, but Tian Heung Hee did not accept the edict.

古文：壬子，充州复为果州。
现代文：十八日，充州重又恢复为果州。
English: On the 18th, the status of Chenzhou was changed back to that of Guozhou.

古文：癸丑。田承嗣盗取洺州，又破卫州。
现代文：十九日，田承嗣盗取州，又攻破了卫州。
English: On the 19th, Tian Cheng He stole the state and broke through the state of Weizhou.

古文：二月乙丑，盗杀卫州刺史薛雄。
现代文：二月一日，盗贼杀害了卫州刺史薛雄。
English: On February 1, thieves killed Wei Zhou's assistant, Xue Xiong.

古文：丙寅，罢辰、锦、溪、奖、溆五州经略使，复隶黔中。
现代文：二日，罢免了辰、锦、溪、奖、溆五州经略使。让五州重新隶属黔中。
English: On the second day, the five provincial economic commissioners of Chen, Jin, Xixi, Shou and Handan were dismissed, and the five provinces were re-subordinated to Handan.

古文：辛未，制第四子述封睦王，充岭南节度度支营田、王府经略观察处置等大使。
现代文：七日，皇上下令，第四个儿子李述封为睦王，充任岭南节度使、度支使、营田使、王府经略使、观察处置使。
English: On the seventh day, the emperor issued an order, and the fourth son, Li Shufeng, was appointed as King Mugu, and was appointed as the Lingnan Festival Envoy, Doushi Envoy, Yingtian Envoy, Wangfujing Envoy, and Observation and Disposition Envoy.

古文：第五子逾可封郴王，充渭北鄜坊等州节度大使。
现代文：第五个儿子李逾封为郴王，并充任渭北、坊等州节度大使。
English: The fifth son, Li Chaofeng, became the king of Shandong, and served as the ambassador of the state festival in Shandong North, Fang and other provinces.

古文：第六子连封恩王。
现代文：第六个儿子李连封为恩王。
English: The sixth son, Li Lianfeng, became the King of Grace.

古文：第七子韩王迥可充汴宋节度大使。
现代文：第七个儿子韩王迥充任汴宋节度大使。
English: The seventh son, Han Wang Yuchong, served as the ambassador to the Song Dynasty.

古文：第八子遘可封鄜王。
现代文：第八个儿子李遘封为王。
English: The eighth son, Li Yufeng, became king.

古文：第十三子造封忻王，充昭义节度大使。
现代文：第十三个儿子李造封为忻王，并充任昭义节度大使。
English: The thirteenth son, Li Zoufeng, became the king of Shanshan and served as the ambassador of the Shouyi Festival.

古文：十七子遹封循王。
现代文：第十四个儿子李逻封为韶王。
English: The fourteenth son, Li Luo, was crowned the Dragon King.

古文：十八子通封恭王。
现代文：第十五个儿子李运封为嘉王。
English: The fifteenth son, Li Yunfeng, became King Jia.

古文：十九子达封原王。
现代文：第十六个儿子李遇封为端王。
English: The sixteenth son, Li Yufu, was crowned the Dragon King.

古文：二十子逸封雅王。
现代文：第十七个儿子李封为循王。
English: The seventeenth son, Li Feng, became King Xu.

古文：并可开府仪同三司，不出阁。
现代文：都适合任开府仪同三司，但都不实际任开府仪同三司之实职。
English: All of them are suitable for holding the office of Kaifu Yi and the three departments, but none of them actually hold the office of Kaifu Yi and the three departments.

古文：丙子，以华州刺史李承昭为相州刺史。知昭义兵马留后。时田承嗣尽盗入相、卫所管四州之地，自署长吏。
现代文：十二日，以华州刺史李承昭为相州刺史，主持昭义兵马留后的工作，当时田承嗣已经全部劫掠了相州、卫州所管辖的田州之地，自己任命地位较高的官吏。
English: On the twelfth day, Li Chengzhao, the historian of Huazhou, was appointed as the historian of Xiangzhou to preside over the work after the soldiers and horses of Zhao Yi left. At that time, Tian Chengzhe had already plundered all the land of Tianzhou under the jurisdiction of Xiangzhou and Weizhou, and appointed high-ranking officials himself.

古文：是日河阳军乱，逐城使常休明，迫牙将王惟恭为留后，军士大掠数日，休明奔东都。
现代文：这天河阳军乱，驱逐了城使常休明，逼迫牙将王惟恭为留后，军士大肆抢掠数天。常休明奔逃到东都。
English: On this day, there was a mutiny in the Kawayan army, and after expelling the city envoy, Jokyu Ming, and forcing the commander, Wang Weigong, to stay behind, the sergeants plundered and pillaged for several days. Jokyu Ming fled to the eastern capital.

古文：甲申，以平卢淄青节度观察海运押新罗渤海两蕃等使、检校工部尚书、青州刺史李正己检校尚书左仆射；前陇右节度副使、陇州刺史马燧为商州刺史，充本州防御使。
现代文：二十六日，以平卢、淄青节度使、观察使、海运押新罗使、押渤海使、检校工部尚书、青州刺史李正己为检校尚书左仆射；前任陇右节度副使、陇州刺史马燧为商州刺史，充任本州防御使。
English: On the 26th, with Pinglu, Handan and Qingdao as the dispatching envoys, observation envoys, shipping envoys to Silla, and Handan and Qingdao as the dispatching envoys, Shang Shu of the inspection department and Li Zhengyi of Qingdao as the dispatching envoys left and right; the former deputy envoy of Handan and Qingdao as the dispatching envoys, and Handan and Qingdao as the dispatching envoys of Shangzhou, he served as the defense envoy of this state.

古文：三月甲午，陕州军乱，逐观察使李国清，纵兵大掠。
现代文：三月一日，陕州军大乱，驱逐观察使李国清，放纵唆使军队大肆抢掠。
English: On March 1, the Shaanxi army rioted. Li Guoqing was forced to expel the observers and encouraged the troops to loot and pillage.

古文：国清卑词遍拜将士，方免祸，一夕而定。
现代文：李国清低三下四遍拜所有将士，方才免祸，一晚上才安定。
English: Li Guoqing bowed low three times and bowed four times to all the soldiers, only then was he spared from disaster, and only then was he stable overnight.

古文：乙巳，薛崿、常休明至阙下，素服待罪。
现代文：十二日，薛、常休明到了宫阙之下，身穿白色素衣待罪朝廷。
English: On the twelfth day, Xue and Changhui went to the palace, dressed in white plain clothes, and waited for the court.

古文：丁未，以左散骑常侍孟皞为华州刺史，充潼关防御使。
现代文：十四日，以左散骑常侍孟白皋为华州刺史，充任潼关防御使。
English: On the 14th, Meng Baiyao, a left-handed horseback rider and a regular attendant, was appointed as the official historian of Huazhou and served as the defense envoy of Shaoguan.

古文：庚戌，荧惑入壁垒。
现代文：十七日，荧惑星进入壁垒星座。
English: On the 17th, the fluorescent planet entered the barrier constellation.

古文：四月，太常寺奏：诸州府所用斗秤，当寺给铜斗秤，州府依样制造而行，从之。
现代文：四月，太常寺上奏：各州府所用斗和秤，应当是太常寺给的铜斗秤，各州府应该依照样品制造使用施行。
English: In April, Taejon-ji Temple announced that the scales and buckets used by prefectural governments should be the bronze scales and buckets given by Taejon-ji Temple, and that prefectural governments should use the scales and buckets according to the samples made.

古文：乙丑，制：魏博节度使、开府仪岵司、太尉、检校尚书左仆射、同中书门下平章事、魏州大都督府长史、上柱国、雁门郡王田承嗣可贬永州刺史。
现代文：皇上听从了。三日，皇上下诏令：魏博节度使、开府仪同三司、太尉、检校尚书左仆射、同中书门下平章事、魏州大都督府长史、上柱国、雁门郡王田承嗣贬为永州刺史。
English: The emperor obeyed. On the third day, the emperor issued an imperial edict: Wei Bo festival envoy, Kaifu ceremony with three divisions, captain, school inspection Shang Shuxu Zuo Shuai, with the middle school door down Ping Zhangji, the governor of the governor of Wei Province, Shangzhuo Province, and Wang Tian Chengzhi of Ganmen County were reduced to Yongzhou sashimi.

古文：仍诏河东、镇冀、幽州、淄青、淮西、滑毫、汴宋、泽潞、河阳道出师进讨。
现代文：仍旧诏令河东、镇冀、幽州、淄青、淮西、滑亳、汴宋、泽潞、河阳道出军队讨伐田承嗣。
English: The imperial edict still ordered troops from the provinces of Hedong, Zhenji, Yuzhou, Jiaqing, Huaxi, Nanzhuang, Jiaosong, Zeyu and Heyang to fight against the felling of rice fields.

古文：甲申，大雨雹，暴风拔树，飘屋瓦，落鸱吻，人震死者十之二，京畿损稼者七县。
现代文：二十二日，下大雨，下大冰雹，暴风拔起树木，吹走了屋瓦，吹落了屋脊上的装饰物，人们被震死者十分之二，京城附近庄稼受损的有七个县。
English: On the 22nd, there was heavy rain, large hailstones, and the storm uprooted trees, blew away roof tiles, and blew down decorations on the roof. Two-tenths of the people were killed by the earthquake, and crops near the capital were damaged in seven counties.

古文：五月乙未，田承嗣部将霍荣国以磁州归。
现代文：五月三日，田承嗣的部将霍荣国带领磁州归附。
English: On May 3rd, Tian Chengzhi's troops led by Huo Rong Guo annexed Magnetized Prefecture.

古文：癸卯，剑南置昌州。
现代文：十一日，在剑南设置昌州。
English: On the 11th, Changzhou was set up in Jianan.

古文：罢两都贡举，都集上都，停童子科。
现代文：撤销东都、西都的科举考试，全部集中到上都考试，停止童子科。
English: Revoke the East and West Capital Examinations, concentrate them all on the Shanghai Capital Examinations, and stop the children's department.

古文：六月辛未，田承承嗣遣其党裴志清攻围冀州，为李宝臣所败。
现代文：六月九日，田承嗣派遣他的党羽裴志清包围攻打冀州，被李宝臣击败。
English: On June 9, Tian Chengzhi sent his followers to encircle and attack Jizhou, and was defeated by Li Baochen.

古文：秋七月己未。户部尚书暢璀卒。
现代文：秋七月二十八日，户部尚书畅璀去世。
English: On the 28th day of the 7th month of autumn, the head of the household, Shangshu Changyao, passed away.

古文：杭州大风，海水翻潮，溺州民五千家，船千艘。
现代文：杭州起大风，海水翻起潮水，漂死杭州民众五千家，漂没船只一千艘。
English: A gale blew up in Hangzhou, the sea turned tidal, and five thousand people in Hangzhou were swept away, and a thousand ships were lost.

古文：八月丁卯，田承嗣上表请束身归朝。
现代文：八月六日，田承嗣上表请求捆缚自己归附朝廷请罪。
English: On August 6th, Tian Chengzhi went to the court and asked to be bound to the court to plead guilty.

古文：戊子夜，月入太微。
现代文：二十七日夜，月亮进入太微星座。
English: On the evening of the 27th, the moon entered the faint constellation.

古文：己丑，田承嗣将卢子期攻磁州。
现代文：二十八日，田承嗣的部将卢子期攻打磁州。
English: On the 28th, Tian Chengzhi's army led by Lu Ziqi attacked Magengzhou.

古文：九月戊戌，荆南节度使卫伯玉来朝。
现代文：九月七日，荆南节度使卫伯玉前来朝见。
English: On September 7, the Jingnan Festival made Wei Boyu come to see the emperor.

古文：月晕，荧惑犯昴、五车、参、东井等星。
现代文：十一日，宽恕京城被关押囚犯。十七日，回纥兵在市场上白昼杀人，官吏将他们捕捉住，关押在万年监狱。
English: On the 17th, Uighur soldiers killed people in the market in broad daylight. Officials caught them and detained them in the 10,000-year prison.

古文：癸丑，吐蕃寇陇州，凤翔李抱玉击之。
现代文：回纥的首领赤心手持兵器进入县城，抢劫囚犯而出，砍伤了监狱官员。二十二日，吐蕃入侵陇州，凤翔府事李抱玉将他击退。
English: The leader of the Uighurs, Chikshin, entered the county seat with a weapon in his hand, robbed prisoners, and slashed prison officials. On the 22nd, the Tibetans invaded Zhangzhou, and the Fengxiang prefect Li Baoyu repelled him.

古文：戊午，幽州节度使硃泚镇奉天。
现代文：二十七日，幽州节度使朱氵此镇守奉天。
English: On the 27th, the Yuzhou Festival made Zhu Xi this town guard Feng Tian.

古文：冬十月辛酉日，日有蚀之。
现代文：冬十月一日，有日蚀。
English: In winter, on October 1st, there is a solar eclipse.

古文：癸亥，以商州刺史马燧检校左散骑常侍、河阳三城使。
现代文：三日，以商州刺史马燧任检校左散骑常侍、河阳三城使。
English: On the third day, he was appointed as the Left Sanzhong riding attendant of the inspection school and the envoy of the three cities of Hebei and Yangzhou.

古文：甲子，昭义节度使李承昭与卢子期战于磁州清水县，大破之，生擒子期以献。
现代文：四日，昭义节度使李承昭与卢子期在磁州清水县大战，大破敌军，活捉卢子期献给朝廷。
English: On the 4th, the Shouyi Festival made Li Chengzhao and Lu Ziqi fight a great battle in Qingshui County, Gansu Province. They defeated the enemy army and captured Lu Ziqi alive and presented him to the imperial court.

古文：丙寅，贵妃独孤氏薨，追赠曰贞懿皇后。

English: On the 6th, Guifei Doko died, and was posthumously given the title of Empress Zhenyao.

English: On the seventeenth day, Lu Tsigong invaded Guangzhou, captured Brother Shu alive, cut off his head and came to contribute.

古文：十一年春正月庚寅朔，田承嗣上表请罪。

English: The first day of the first month of spring in the eleventh year was the new moon day, and Tian Chengzhi went to appeal for punishment.

English: On the third day, the emperor sent Duya, the doctor of deliberation, to pacify Weizhou, and agreed to let him reform.

古文：辛亥。剑南节度使崔宁奏大破吐蕃二十万，斩首万级，生擒首领一千一百五十人，献于阙下。
现代文：二十二日，剑南节度使崔宁上奏说，大破吐蕃军二十万，斩敌首一万个，活捉敌首领一千一百五十人，献到朝廷。
English: On the 22nd, the Jian'nan Festival made Cui Ning make a report, saying that he had defeated 200,000 Tuyun troops, decapitated 10,000 enemies, captured 150 enemy leaders alive, and presented them to the imperial court.

古文：二月癸亥，荆南节度使卫伯玉卒于京师。

English: On February 5, Jingnan Festival, Wei Boyu passed away in Beijing.

古文：戊子，河阳军复乱，大掠三日，监军使冉廷兰率兵斩其乱首。方定。
现代文：三月一日，河阳军重又大乱，大肆抢劫三天，监军使冉廷兰率兵斩了动乱的首领，大乱才平定。
English: On the first day of March, there was heavy fighting and chaos in Kheyang, and there was large-scale looting for three days. The leader of the turmoil was beheaded by the supervising army commander, Ran Tinglan, and the turmoil was finally quelled.

古文：夏四月戊午朔。
现代文：夏四月一日是朔日。
English: In summer, the first day of April falls on a Saturday.

古文：己卯，以前淮南节度使、阳州大都督府长史、御史大夫张延赏为江陵尹、兼御史大夫充荆南节度使。
现代文：二十二日，以前任淮南节度使、扬州大都护府长史、御史大夫张延赏为江陵尹、兼御史大夫，充任荆南节度使。
English: On the 22nd, Zhang Yanbo, the former Huainan Festival Envoy, Yangzhou Metropolis Protectorate Chief Historian and Grand Historian, was awarded as Jiangling Yin, also Grand Historian, and appointed as Jingnan Festival Envoy.

古文：五月癸巳，以永平军节度使李勉为汴州刺史，充汴宋等八州节度观察留后，时汴将李灵耀专杀濮州刺史孟鉴，北连田承嗣。故命勉兼领汴州。
现代文：五月七日，以永平军节度使李勉为汴州刺史，充任汴、宋等八州节度使、观察留后。当时汴州将李灵耀擅自杀害濮州刺史孟鉴，往北勾结田承嗣，所以命令李勉兼任汴州刺史的职衔。
English: On May 7, at the Yongping Army Festival, Li Tsuen was appointed as the chief historian of Bozhou, and served as the chief historian and observer of eight state festivals such as the Song Dynasty and the Song Dynasty. At that time, Bozhou ordered Li Lingyao to commit suicide without permission, kill the chief historian of Bozhou, Meng Jian, and collude with Tian Hei He to the north, so Li Tsuen was also ordered to serve as the chief historian of Bozhou.

古文：授灵耀濮州刺史，灵耀不受诏。
现代文：皇上授予李灵耀为濮州刺史，李灵耀不接受命令。
English: The emperor awarded Li Lingyao to write the history of Zhangzhou, but Li Lingyao did not accept the order.

古文：六月戊戌，以李灵耀为汴州刺史，充节度留后。

English: On June 2nd, Li Lingyao was appointed as the chief historian of Zhangzhou, leaving Mao as the head of the festival.

English: On the evening of the 3rd day of the 7th month of autumn, torrential rain fell, the water depth of the flat land was one foot, the ditch was full, and 1200 houses were damaged.
