English: On the 29th, he ordered Li Zhongchen of Huaxi, Li Mian of Nanzhou, and Ma Jun of Heyang to lead the troops of the three towns to fight against him.

English: On the twelfth day of the eighth month, a very white star streaked across the sky.

English: On September 11, the army of Li Zhongchen and others marched into Zhengzhou, and Li Lingyao's troops approached to fight.

English: On the first day of October in winter, the army of Li Zhongchen and others defeated the bandits in Zhongmuda, continued to march and attack, and defeated the bandits outside the city of Zhangzhou, and then continued to attack.

古文：乙丑，承嗣遣侄悦率兵三万援灵耀。

English: On the 19th, Tian Chengxi sent his nephew Tian Yue and 30,000 soldiers to rescue Li Lingyao.

古文：丙午，淮西、河阳之师合击田悦营，其众大败，悦脱身北走。

English: On the 22nd, the armies of Huaxi and Heyang rallied to attack Tian Yue's camp. Tian Yue's army was soundly defeated, and Tian Yue escaped to the north.

English: When Li Lingyao heard that Tian Yue had failed, he abandoned the city and fled.

古文：汴州平。丁未，滑将杜如江生擒灵耀而献。

古文：昭义节度使李承昭搞表称疾，以泽潞行军司马李抱真权知磁、邢兵马留后。

古文：庚午，左降官永州刺史田承嗣复授魏博节度使，余官并如故。承嗣侄悦、子绾绪纶并复旧官。

English: On the 18th, the demoted official Yongzhou Shishi Tian Chengzhi re-awarded him Wei Bo Festival to make him a post, and the remaining posts were the same as before. Tian Chengzhi's nephew Tian Yue, son Tian Yao, Tian Xiu, and Tian Yao all resumed their former official posts.

English: On the 28th, the prime minister, Yuan Zai, and the minister of justice, Wang Xingde, went to the prison and ordered the official, Shangshu Liu Jie, to interrogate them.

古文：辛巳，制：中书侍郎、平章事元载赐自尽，门下侍郎、平章事王缙贬括州刺史。

English: On the 29th, the emperor issued an imperial decree: Zhongshu's attendant, Pingzhang Jiji, committed suicide, and his subordinate attendant, Pingzhang Jiji Wang, was relegated to the status of bracketed history.

古文：夏四月壬午，以朝议大夫、守太常卿、兼修国史杨绾为中书侍郎，尚书礼部郎、集贤院学士常衮为门下侍郎，并同中书门下平章事。
现代文：夏四月一日，以朝议大夫、守太常卿、兼修撰国史杨绾为中书侍郎，尚书礼部侍郎、集贤院学士常衮为门下侍郎，并都任同中书门下平章事。
English: On the first day of the fourth month of the summer, with the doctor of the Imperial Court Council, the governor of the Imperial Court, and the concurrently studying and compiling the national history Yang Xi as the junior attendant, the junior attendant of the Shoshu Rite Department, and the junior attendant of the scholar of the Jixian Academy, and all of them were appointed as junior subordinate officers of the same junior attendant.

古文：癸未，以右庶子潘炎为礼部侍郎。
现代文：二日，以右庶子潘炎为礼部侍郎。
English: On the second day, he appointed his son-in-law, Pan Yan, as a ceremonial attendant.

古文：贬吏部侍郎杨炎为道州司马，元载党也。
现代文：贬吏部侍郎杨炎为道州司马，因为他是元载一党。
English: Yang Yan, the attendant of the Ministry of Decrees, is the Sima of Daozhou, because he was a member of the party in the Yuan Dynasty.

古文：谏议大夫、知制诰韩洄王定包佶徐璜，户部侍郎赵纵，大理少卿裴翼，太常少卿王紞，起居舍人韩会等十余人，皆坐元载贬官也。
现代文：谏议大夫、知制诰韩洄、王定、包佶、徐璜，户部侍郎赵纵，大理少卿裴翼，太常少卿王，起居舍人韩会等十多人，都由于元载的罪而牵连犯罪贬官也。
English: More than a dozen people, including 议大夫,知制韩,王定,包,徐,户部侍郎赵纵,大理少卿裴翼,太常少卿王,起居舍人韩会 and so on, were implicated in the crime and demoted due to the crime of Yuan Zai.

古文：给事中杜亚使魏州，赐田承嗣铁券。
现代文：给事中杜亚出使魏州，赐给田承嗣世代享受特权的铁券。
English: In the middle of the matter, Duya sent an envoy to Weizhou, and gave Tian Chengzhe's generation the privilege of iron coupons.

古文：癸巳，以前秘书监李揆为睦州刺史。
现代文：十二日，以前任秘书监的李揆为睦州刺史。
English: On the 12th, the former secretary supervisor, Li Xuan, made history in Mutsu.

古文：揆故宰相，为元载所忌，二十年流落丐食江湖间，载诛，方得为郡。
现代文：李揆原来是宰相，由于被元载猜忌，二十年来流落江湖乞讨食物，形同乞丐，元载被杀后，才能重新任为郡守。
English: Li Yan was originally the prime minister, but because he was suspected by Yuan Zai, he wandered around for twenty years begging for food, like a beggar. Only after Yuan Zai was killed could he be reappointed as county governor.

古文：又召颜真卿于湖州，亦载所忌斥外也。
现代文：皇上又从湖州召回颜真卿，他也是遭元载猜忌而被贬斥到外地去的。
English: The emperor also recalled Yan Zhenqing from Huzhou. He also suffered from the suspicion of the Yuan Zai and was relegated to other places.

古文：乙未，月掩心前星。
现代文：十四日，月亮遮掩了心前星。
English: On the 14th, the moon obscured the foreground star.

古文：丁酉，西川破吐蕃于望汉城，擒蕃将大笼官论器然以献。
现代文：十六日，西川在望汉城攻破了吐蕃，活捉吐蕃大将大笼官论器然献给朝廷。
English: On the 16th, Nishikawa defeated the Tujue in the city of Bongseong, captured the Tujue alive, and presented the Tujue to the imperial court.

古文：壬寅，以前商州刺史乌崇福为安南都护、本营经略使。
现代文：二十一日，以前任商州刺史乌崇福为安南都护、本管经略使。
English: On the twenty-first day of the month, Wu Chongfu, the former governor of Shangzhou, was appointed as the guardian of the capital of Annan and the special envoy of the governor.

古文：渤海、奚、契丹、室韦、靺鞨并遣使朝贡。
现代文：渤海、奚、契丹、室韦、革末革曷等国都派遣使者前来朝贡。
English: Countries such as Bohai, Min, Khitan, Murowe, and Qamdo Qamdo all sent envoys to pay tribute.

古文：己酉，加京官料钱，文武班诸司共二千七百九十六员，文官一千八五十四员，武官九百四十二员，岁加给一十五万六千贯，并旧给凡二十六万贯。
现代文：二十八日，皇上加给京官薪俸以外的料钱，文武两班各司共二千七百九十六名官员，其中文官一千八百五十四员，武官九百四十二员，每年加给一十五万六千贯，连旧有料钱一共二十六万贯。
English: On the 28th, the emperor increased the salary of officials in Beijing to a total of 2,796 officials, including 1,854 civil servants and 942 military attaches. The annual salary was increased to 156,000 kun, with the old salary amounting to 260,000 kun.

古文：以关内副元帅、兵马使浑瑊兼邠州刺史。
现代文：以关内副元帅、兵马使浑王咸兼任州刺史。
English: In addition to being the vice-marshal of Kwanai and the commander of the troops and horses, Hun Wangxian also served as the prefectural governor.

古文：五月辛亥。罢天下州团练守捉使名。
现代文：五月一日，撤销天下各州团练守捉使的职务名称。
English: On May 1st, the job title of the world's top regimental training officer was revoked.

古文：甲寅，诸道邸务在上都名曰留后，改为进奏院。
现代文：四日，各道在上都的官邸负责的职务名叫留后，改为进奏院。
English: On the 4th, the official residence in Shangdu that each province was responsible for was renamed "Zuruo" and changed to "Jinsoin."

古文：丙辰夜，月入太微。
现代文：六日夜，月亮进入太微星座。
English: On the evening of the sixth day, the moon entered the faint constellation.

古文：辛酉，贬刑部尚书王昂连州刺史，昂至万州卒。
现代文：十一日，贬刑部尚书王昂为连州刺史，王昂到万州时去世。
English: On the 11th day of the month, Wang Ang, a member of the Penal Correction Department, wrote a history of Lianzhou. Wang Ang died when he arrived in Wanzhou.

古文：庚午，敕毁元载祖、父坟，剖棺弃骸，焚毁私庙主于大宁里。
现代文：二十日，皇上命令毁掉元载的祖父、父亲的坟墓，剖开棺木，弃掉尸骨，在大宁里烧毁私家庙宇神主。
English: On the 20th, the emperor ordered the destruction of the tomb of Yuan Zai's grandfather and father, opened the coffin, discarded the bones, and burned the private temple of the god in Daningli.

古文：甲戌，以前安南都护张伯仪为广州刺史、兼御史大夫，充岭南节度使。
现代文：二十四日，以前任安南都护张伯仪为广州刺史、兼任御史大夫，并充任岭南节度使。
English: On the 24th, Zhang Bo Yi, the former Annan Metropolitan Protector, was appointed as the Guangzhou Historian, concurrently serving as the Imperial Historian, and acting as the Lingnan Festival Envoy.

古文：六月癸巳，时小旱，上斋居祈祷，圣体不康，是日不视朝。
现代文：六月十三日，当时有小小干旱，皇上更衣、沐浴、吃素、独居而祈祷。皇上身体不适，这天不上朝。
English: On June 13th, when there was a small drought, the emperor changed clothes, bathed, ate vegetarian, lived alone and prayed. The emperor was unwell and did not go to the court that day.

古文：秋七月戊午，罢润州丹阳军、苏州长洲军。
现代文：秋七月九日，撤销润州丹阳军、苏州长洲军。
English: On the 9th day of the 7th month of autumn, the Danyang Army of Rongzhou and the Changzhou Army of Suzhou were revoked.

古文：己巳，中书侍郎、同中书门下平章事、集贤殿崇文馆大学士、兼修国史杨绾卒。
现代文：二十日，中书侍郎、同中书门下平章事、集贤殿崇文馆大学士、兼修国史杨绾去世。
English: On the 20th day of the month, Yang Xi, the attendant of the Chinese classics, the disciple of the same Chinese classics, the disciple of the same Chinese classics, the disciple of the same Chinese classics, the disciple of the same Chinese classics, the disciple of the same Chinese classics, the disciple of the same Chinese classics, the disciple of the same Chinese classics, the disciple of the same Chinese classics, the disciple of the same Chinese classics.

古文：八月癸巳，赐东川节度使鲜于叔明姓李氏。
现代文：八月十四日，赐东川节度使鲜于叔明姓李。
English: On August 14th, the Dongchuan Festival was given to Shun Yu Shu Ming surnamed Li.

古文：癸卯，宰臣让赐食。
现代文：二十四日，宰相对皇上赐给的食物谦让辞谢。
English: On the 24th, the head steward humbly declined the food given by the emperor.

古文：先是元载、王缙辅政，每日赐食，因为故事。
现代文：先前元载、王缙辅政，皇上每天赐给食物，因此成为旧例。
English: Previously, the emperor gave food to the emperor every day during the reign of Wang Xiufu, so it became an old case.

古文：至是，常衮等上表云： 飧钱已多，更颁御膳，胡颜自安，乞停赐食。 
现代文：至此，常衮等人上表曰： 夕食之钱已经很多，又颁赐皇上御用之食，哪有颜面安心享受，请求停止赐食。 
English: At this point, Tsuneyoshi and others came up to the table and said, "There is already a lot of money for dinner, and the emperor's food has been given out. How can you enjoy it without shame? We request that you stop giving out food."

古文：从之。
现代文：皇上依从了。
English: I followed his advice.

古文：甲辰，以湖州刺史颜真卿为刑部尚书。
现代文：二十五日，以湖州刺史颜真卿为刑部尚书。
English: On the 25th, Yan Zhenqing of Huzhou Province was appointed as the head of the Criminal Law Department.

古文：乙巳，以久雨宥常参百僚，不许御史点班。
现代文：二十六日，因为长期下雨，原谅经常参见皇上的百官，不许御史点班点名。
English: On the twenty-sixth day, because of the long-term rain, forgive the hundred officials who often see the emperor, and do not allow the history class to call names.

古文：九月乙卯，许以庶人礼葬元载。
现代文：九月七日，皇上同意以平民之礼遇安葬元载。
English: On September 7, the Emperor agreed to be buried with the courtesy of a commoner.

古文：辛酉，以泾原节度副使段秀实为四镇北庭行营、泾原郑颍等节度使。
现代文：十三日，以泾原节度副使段秀实为四镇、北庭行营、泾原、郑、颍等州节度使。
English: On the 13th, Duan Xiushi, deputy envoy of the Xingyuan Festival, was appointed as the delegate of the Xingyuan Festival in four towns, Beiting Xingyuan, Xingyuan, Zheng and Handan.

古文：庚午，吐蕃寇坊州，掠党项羊马而去。
现代文：二十二日，吐蕃入侵坊州，抢夺党项羊、马而去。
English: On the 22nd, Tubo invaded Fangzhou, robbed the party's sheep and horses and left.

古文：是秋，宋、亳、陈、滑等州水。
现代文：这年秋天，宋、亳、陈、滑等州发大水。
English: In the autumn of that year, Song, Min, Chen, Nanning and other prefectures were hit by floods.

古文：冬十月丁亥，户部待郎、判度支韩滉言解县两池生瑞盐，乃置祠，号宝应灵庆池。
现代文：冬十月九日，户部侍郎兼任度支郎韩说解县有两个池子生出吉祥之盐，于是设置祠堂，号曰宝应灵庆池。
English: On the 9th of October in winter, the head of the household, who also served as the head of the household, Han said that there were two ponds in the county that produced auspicious salt, so the ancestral hall was set up, called Baoying Lingqing Pond.

古文：壬寅夜，月掩昴，又入太微。
现代文：二十四日夜，月亮遮掩昴星，又进入太微星座。
English: On the night of the twenty-fourth day, the moon covered the bright star and entered the faint constellation.

古文：乙巳，以滑州牙将刘洽为宋州刺史。
现代文：二十七日，以滑州牙将刘洽为宋州刺史。
English: On the 27th, the history of Songzhou was written with the help of Liu Cai, the leader of the Nanzhou Fang.

古文：京兆尹黎干奏水损田三万一千顷。
现代文：京兆尹黎干上奏说，大水损田三万一千顷。
English: Jing Zhaoyun Li Gan reported that the flood had damaged 31,000 hectares of fields.

古文：度支使韩滉奏所损不多。
现代文：度支使韩上奏说所损不多。
English: There is not much damage to be said about the degree of support for South Korea.

古文：兼渭南令刘藻曲附滉，亦云部内田不损。
现代文：兼任渭南令刘灌附会韩，也说渭南内田没有损失。
English: Liu Guanzhong, who also serves as the commander of South Shandong Province, also said that there was no loss to South Shandong Province.

古文：差御史赵计检渭南田，亦附滉云不损。
现代文：皇上派遣御史赵计检验渭南田，也附会韩说不曾损失。
English: The emperor dispatched the imperial historian Zhao Jie to inspect the southern fields, and the Han Dynasty also said that there was no loss.

古文：上曰： 水旱咸均，不宜渭南独免。 
现代文：皇上说 ：水灾旱灾各地都应一样，不应该渭南独自免除灾害。 
English: The emperor said, "Floods and droughts should be the same everywhere, and southern Shandong should not be exempted from disasters.

古文：复命御史硃敖检之，渭南损田三千顷。
现代文：再次命令御史朱敖检验，结果报告说，渭南损失田地三千顷。
English: He once again ordered the inspector Zhu Xi to inspect, and the results reported that the loss of fields in southern Anhui amounted to three thousand hectares.

古文：上叹息曰： 县令职在字人，不损亦宜称损，损而不闻，岂有恤隐之意耶！
现代文：皇上叹息道： 县令的职责在于爱人，没有损失田地也应说损失，损失田地然而还不上报，难道有同情怜恤百姓之意吗？ 
English: The emperor sighed, "The duty of a county magistrate is to love his people. If there is no loss of farmland, it should be said to be a loss. However, if there is a loss of farmland, it is not reported. Is there any sympathy or mercy for the people?

古文：刘藻、赵计皆贬官。
现代文：刘藻、赵计都贬官。
English: Liu Mo and Zhao Jie were both demoted.

古文：十一月癸丑，太白临哭星。
现代文：十一月五日，太白星驾临大哭星之上。
English: On November 5th, Taibai Xing rode on the top of the Big Weeping Star.

古文：乙卯夜，月入羽林。
现代文：七日夜，月亮进入羽林星。
English: On the night of the seventh day, the moon entered the constellation of the Feathered Forest.

古文：癸酉，以右散骑常侍萧昕为工阅尚书。
现代文：二十五日，以右散骑常侍萧昕为工部尚书。
English: On the twenty-fifth day, the right horseback riding attendant Xiao Wei was appointed as the official of the work department.

古文：刑部尚书颜真卿献所著《韵海镜源》三百六十卷。
现代文：刑部尚书颜真卿献上所著《韵海镜源》三百六十卷。
English: Shang Shuxuan Zhenqing of the Criminal Investigation Department presented 360 volumes of his book "Rhyme Sea Mirror Source."

古文：十二月丁亥，西川崔宁奏于西山破吐蕃十万，斩首八千，生擒九百人。
现代文：十二月九日，西川崔宁上奏说，在西山攻破吐蕃兵十万人，斩敌首八千人，活捉九百人。
English: On December 9, Cui Ning of Xichuan reported that he had defeated 100,000 Tuoba soldiers in Xishan, beheaded 8,000 enemy soldiers, and captured 900 alive.

古文：己亥，天下仙洞灵迹禁樵捕。
现代文：二十一日，天下仙洞和神灵遗迹严禁砍柴捕捉野兽鱼类。
English: On the twenty-first day, it is strictly forbidden to cut firewood to catch wild fish in the world of fairy caves and relics of gods.

古文：庚子，以幽州节度使硃泚兼陇右节度副大使，权知河西、泽潞行营兵马事。
现代文：二十二日，以幽州节度使朱氵此兼任陇右节度副大使，暂代主持河西、泽、潞行营兵马事。
English: On the 22nd, with the Yuzhou Festival, Zhu Xi was concurrently appointed as the vice ambassador of the Shiyu Festival, temporarily presiding over the soldiers and horses of the Hexi, Ze and Minhang camps.

古文：京兆尹请修六门堰，许之。
现代文：京兆尹请求修建六门堰，皇上同意了。
English: Jing Zhaoyun requested the construction of the Six-Gate Weir, and the emperor agreed.

古文：十三年春正月戊申朔。
现代文：大历十三年春正月一日是朔日。
English: The first day of the first month of spring in the 13th year of the lunar calendar is the New Year's Day.

古文：辛酉，坏白渠碾硙八十余所，以夺农溉田也。
现代文：十四日，破坏白渠机械水磨八十多处，因为它们夺取了农业灌溉。
English: On the 14th, more than 80 Baiquan mechanical water mills were destroyed, because they seized agricultural irrigation.

古文：壬戌，刑部尚书、鲁郡公颜真卿三抗章乞致仁，不允。
现代文：十五日，刑部尚书、鲁郡公颜真卿三次极力上表章请求辞官，皇上不许。
English: On the 15th, Shang Shu of the Criminal Investigation Department and Gongyan Zhenqing of Lu County went to the emperor three times to ask for his resignation, but the emperor would not allow it.

古文：淄青节度使李正己请附属籍，从之。
现代文：淄青节度使李正己请求附到宗族名册上，皇上同意了。
English: The Emperor agreed to Li Zhengji's request to add him to the family register.

古文：戊辰，回纥寇太原，鲍防与之战，我师不利。
现代文：二十一日，回纥入侵太原，鲍防与回纥作战，我军不利。
English: On the twenty-first day, the Uighurs invaded Taiyuan, Bao Bao fought with the Uighurs, and our army was at a disadvantage.

古文：硃泚徙封遂宁郡王。
现代文：朱氵此改封为遂宁郡王并迁徙到遂宁去。
English: Zhu Xi changed his title to King of Suining County and moved to Suining.

古文：二月庚辰，代州都督张光晟击回纥，战于羊武谷，破之，北人乃安。
现代文：二月三日，代州都督张光晟打击回纥，在羊武谷大战，打败了回纥军，北方人这才安定。
English: On February 3, Zhang Guangya, the governor of Daizhou, launched a strike against the Uighurs and defeated the Uighur army in the Battle of Yangwu Valley. Only then did the northerners become stable.

古文：己亥，吐蕃寇灵武。
现代文：二十二日，吐蕃入侵灵武。
English: On the 22nd, the Tuoba invaded Lingwu.

古文：甲辰，太仆寺佛堂有小脱空金刚右臂忽有黑汁滴下，以纸承之，色类血。
现代文：二十七日，太仆寺佛堂有小脱空金刚右臂忽然有黑汗滴下，以纸接着，颜色类似血。
English: On the 27th, in the Buddhist hall of the Taipo Temple, there was a sudden drop of black sweat on the right arm of Xiao Zhukong, followed by paper, and the color was similar to blood.

古文：三月甲戌，河阳将士劫回纥辎重，因与相斗，纵兵大掠，久之方定。
现代文：三月二十八日，河阳将士抢劫回纥粮食辎重，因而与回纥相打斗，回纥便放纵士兵大肆抢掠，很久才平定。
English: On March 28th, the soldiers from Hebei robbed the soldiers from Huizhou of a large amount of grain. As a result, they fought with the soldiers from Huizhou. The soldiers from Huizhou indulged in large-scale looting and pillaging, and it took a long time to subdue the situation.

古文：四月丁亥，以浙西观察留后李道昌为苏州刺史、兼御史中丞，充浙西都团练观察使。
现代文：四月十一日，以浙西观察留后李道昌为苏州刺史、兼御史中丞，并充任浙西都团练观察使。
English: On April 11th, Li Daochang, who stayed in western Zhejiang to observe, became the Suzhou chief historian and also the vice-president of history, and served as the observer of the western Zhejiang Duan exercise.

古文：己丑，以前浙西观察使李涵为御史大夫。
现代文：十三日，以前任浙西观察使李涵为御史大夫。
English: On the 13th, Li Han, the former director of the West Zhejiang Observation Station, was appointed as the chief historian.

古文：甲辰，吐蕃寇灵州，朔方留后常谦光击败之。
现代文：二十八日，吐蕃入侵灵州，朔方留后常谦光将他们击败。
English: On the 28th, Tubo invaded Lingshou, and Chang Xianguang defeated them after the Shuo side stayed.

古文：五月戊午，宦官刘清潭赐名忠翼。
现代文：五月十三日，宦官刘清潭被皇上赐名忠翼。
English: On May 13, the eunuch Liu Qingtan was given the title of "loyal wing" by the emperor.

古文：六月戊戌，陇右节度使硃泚于军士赵贵家得猫鼠同乳不相害，笼而献之。
现代文：六月四日，陇右节度使朱氵此在军士赵贵家中看到猫和鼠在一起生养，小猫小鼠不互相侵害的奇事，他将猫和老鼠装在一个笼子里进献给皇上。
English: On the 4th of June, Zhu Xizhe saw a miracle in the house of Sergeant Zhao Gui: a cat and a mouse were raised together, and the kittens and mice did not encroach on each other. He put the cat and mouse in a cage and presented it to the emperor.

古文：秋七月壬子，中书舍人崔祐甫知吏部选事。
现代文：秋七月八日，中书舍人崔佑甫主持吏部科举选拔之事。
English: On the 8th day of the 7th month of autumn, Cui Youfu, the person in charge of Chinese literature, presided over the selection of cadres.

古文：癸丑，剑南节度使崔宁加检校司空，东川李叔明加检校工部尚书。辛未，吐蕃寇盐州、庆州。
现代文：九日，剑南节度使崔宁给予检校司空的加官，东川节度使李叔明给予检校工部尚书的加官，二十七日，吐蕃入侵盐州、庆州。
English: On the 9th, the Jian'nan Festival caused Cui Ning to give the additional post of inspector of schools to Wu, and the Dongchuan Festival caused Li Shuming to give the additional post of inspector of schools to Shang Shu, and on the 27th, Tubo invaded Yanzhou and Gyeongju.

古文：八月甲戌朔，成德军节度使李宝臣抗章请复本姓张氏，从之。
现代文：八月一日是朔日，成德军节度使李宝臣强烈上表请求恢复本姓张氏，皇上同意了。
English: August 1 was the New Year's Day, and the German Army Day made Li Baochen strongly request to restore the original surname Zhang, and the emperor agreed.

古文：冬十月丁酉，葬贞懿皇后于庄陵。
现代文：这年冬十月二十五日，在庄陵安葬贞懿皇后。
English: On October 25th of this winter, Empress Zhengyi was buried in Zhuangling.

古文：十一月丁卯，日长至，有司礼昊天上帝于南郊，上不视朝故也。
现代文：十一月二十五日，冬至日到来，有关官员在南郊祭祀昊天上帝，因为皇上不视朝的原因。
English: On November 25, when the winter solstice arrived, the officials concerned offered sacrifices to Haotian God in the southern suburbs, because the emperor did not consider the reasons for the rise of the North.

古文：十二月丙戌，以吏部尚书刘晏为左仆射，判使如故。以给事中杜亚为洪州刺史、兼御史中丞，充江西观察使。
现代文：十二月十四日，以吏部尚书刘晏为左仆射，并像原来一样兼任节度使，以给事中杜亚为洪州刺史、兼御史中丞、充任江西观察使。
English: On December 14th, Shangshu Liu Jia of the cadre department was appointed as the left-hand man, and, as before, he also served as the delegate to the festival, and Duya, who was in charge of the event, was appointed as the Hongzhou chief historian, and also the chief historian, and served as the Jiangxi observation envoy.

古文：以江西观察使路嗣恭为兵部尚书。
现代文：以江西观察使路嗣恭为兵部尚书。
English: The observation of Jiangxi Province made Lu Shigong become a military strategist.

古文：是岁，郴州黄芩山崩，压死者有数百人。
现代文：这年，郴州黄芩山崩塌，压死数百人。
English: This year, Mount Huangpi in Zhangzhou collapsed, crushing hundreds of people to death.

古文：十四年春正月壬寅朔。
现代文：大历十四年春正月一日是朔日。
English: The first day of the first month of spring in the 14th year of the lunar calendar is New Year's Day.

古文：壬戌，以楚州刺史李泌为澧州刺史。
现代文：二十一日，以楚州刺史李泌为澧州刺史。
English: On the 21st, Li Jie, the Chuzhou stabbing historian, was appointed as the Zhangzhou stabbing historian.

古文：二月癸未，魏博七州节度使、太尉、检校尚书左仆射、同中书门下平章事、魏州大都督府长史田承嗣卒。
现代文：二月十二日，魏博七州节度使、太尉、检校尚书左仆射、同中书门下平章事、魏州大都督府长史田承嗣去世。
English: On February 12th, the Wei Bo seven-state festival envoy, captain, school inspector Shang Shu Zuo Fu Sha, the same middle school student Xia Ping Zhang, and the governor of the Wei State Grand Duchy, Shi Tian Cheng He, passed away.

古文：甲申，以魏博中军兵马使、左司马田悦兼御史中丞，充魏博节度留后。
现代文：十三日，以魏博中军兵马使、左司马田悦兼御史中丞，充任魏博节度留后。
English: On the 13th, Wei Bo's military envoy to the Middle Kingdom of Wei Bo, Zuo Si Ma Tian Yue and Mi Shi Zhongzheng, stayed behind to serve as Wei Bo's commander of the festival.

古文：三月丁未，汴宋节度使李忠臣为麾下将族侄李希烈所逐，忠臣狼狈归朝。
现代文：三月六日，汴宋节度使李忠臣被部下将领族侄李希烈所驱逐，李忠臣狼狈逃回朝廷。
English: On March 6, the Song Dynasty Festival caused Li Zhongcheng to be expelled by his subordinate general's nephew Li Xilai, and Li Zhongcheng fled back to the imperial court.

古文：上以忠臣立功于国，乃授检校司空、同平章事。
现代文：皇上以李忠臣对国有功，乃授予他检校司空、同平章事。
English: The emperor honored Li Zhongchen for his contribution to the state, and awarded him the title of "Inspector of Schools" and "Dongping."

古文：庚戌，以河南尹严郢为京兆尹，河中少尹、知府事赵惠伯为河南尹。
现代文：七日，以河南尹严郢为京兆尹，河中少尹、主持京兆府事的赵惠伯为河南尹。
English: On the 7th, Henan Yin Yanqian was designated as the Beijing Zhaoying, and the minor Yin in the middle of the river and Zhao Huibo, who presided over the affairs of the Beijing Zhaoying, were designated as the Henan Yin.

古文：辛酉，以前容管经略使、容州刺史王翃为河中少尹、知府事。
现代文：二十日，以前任容管经略使、容州刺史王罖为河中少尹、主持河中府事。
English: On the 20th, Wang Yao, who had previously held the position of Deputy Commissioner of the Yungguan Economic Affairs Bureau and Yungju Sashi Wang, was appointed as the Junior Vice-Minister of the Central Government and presided over the affairs of the Central Government.

古文：夏四月癸未，成德军节度使张宝臣复请姓李，从之。
现代文：夏四月十三日，成德军节度使张宝臣再次请求姓李，皇上同意了。
English: On the 13th day of the 4th month of the summer, the Chengde Army Festival made Zhang Baochen once again request the surname Li, and the emperor agreed.

古文：五月癸卯，上不康，至辛亥，不视朝。
现代文：五月三日，皇上有病，直到十一日，不上朝视事。
English: On May 3, the emperor fell ill and did not attend court until the 11th.

古文：北都留守鲍防以北庭归朝。
现代文：北都留守鲍防率北庭归附朝廷。
English: The northern court was annexed to the imperial court with Bao Guo leading the northern court.

古文：辛酉，诏皇太子监国。
现代文：二十一日，诏令皇太子代行国政。
English: On the 21st, the Emperor ordered the Crown Prince to take over state affairs.

古文：是夕，上崩于紫宸之内殿。
现代文：这天晚上，皇上在紫宸宫之内殿去世。
English: On this evening, the Emperor passed away in the inner hall of Shishin Palace.

古文：遗诏皇太子柩前即位。
现代文：皇上遗诏：皇太子在灵柩前即皇帝位。
English: Emperor's last will and testament: The crown prince ascends the throne before the coffin.

古文：壬戌，迁神柩于太极殿，发丧。
现代文：二十二日，把皇上灵柩迁到太极殿，发布丧事。
English: On the 22nd, the emperor's coffin was moved to the Taiji Hall, and the funeral was announced.

古文：八月庚申，群臣上尊谥曰睿文孝武皇帝，庙号代宗。
现代文：八月二十三日，群臣奉上尊谥曰睿文孝武皇帝，庙号代宗。
English: On August 23rd, a group of courtiers paid their respects to Emperor Rui, Emperor Wen, Emperor Wu, and Emperor Daizong.

古文：十月己酉，葬于元陵。
现代文：十月十三日，安葬在元陵。
English: On October 13, he was buried in the original mausoleum.

古文：十二月丁酉，祔于太庙。
现代文：十二月一日，奉代宗神主纎祭于太庙。
English: On the first day of December, the hosannas for the chief god of the Bongdai Sect were held at the Imperial Temple.
